قَالَ عُلَمَاءُ النَّسَبِ، مِنْهُمْ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: اسْمُ سَبَأٍ: عَبْدُ شَمْسِ بْنُ يَشْجُبَ بْنِ يَعْرُبَ بْنِ قَحْطَانَ.

وَإِنَّمَا سُمِّيَ سَبَأً لِأَنَّهُ أَوَّلُ مَنْ سَبَأَ فِي الْعَرَبِ، وَكَانَ يُقَالُ لَهُ: الرَّائِشُ؛ لِأَنَّهُ أَوَّلُ مَنْ غَنِمَ فِي الْغَزْوِ فَأَعْطَى قَوْمَهُ، فَسُمِّي الرَّائِشَ، وَالْعَرَبُ تُسَمِّي الْمَالَ: رِيشًا وَرِيَاشًا. وَذَكَرُوا أَنَّهُ بشَّر بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي زَمَانِهِ الْمُتَقَدِّمِ، وَقَالَ فِي ذَلِكَ شعرًا: سَيَمْلِكُ بَعْدَنَا مُلْكًا عَظيمًا ... نَبيّ لَا يُرَخِّصُ في الحَرَام ...

وَيَْملك بَعْدَه منْهُم مُلُوك ... يدينوه العبادَ بغَير ذَامٍ ...

ويَملك بَعدهم مِنَّا مُلُوك ... يَصير المُلك فينَا باقْتسَام ...

وَيَمْلك بَعَْد قَحْطَان نَبي ... تَقي خَبْتَة خُيْرُ الْأَنَامِ ...

وسُميَ أحْمَدًا يَا لَيْتَ أَنِّي ... أُعَمَّرُ بَعْد مَبْعَثه بِعَامٍ ...

فأعضُده وأَحْبوه بنَصْري ... بكُل مُدَجّج وبكُل رَامٍ ...

مَتَى يَظْهَرْ فَكُونُوا نَاصريه ... وَمَنْ يَلْقَاهُ يُبْلغه سَلامي ...

ذَكَرَ ذَلِكَ الْهَمْدَانِيُّ فِي كِتَابِ "الْإِكْلِيلِ".

وَاخْتَلَفُوا فِي قَحْطَانَ عَلَى ثَلَاثَةِ أَقْوَالٍ:

أَحَدُهَا: أَنَّهُ مِنْ سُلَالَةِ إِرَمَ بْنِ سَامِ بْنِ نُوحٍ، وَاخْتَلَفُوا فِي كَيْفِيَّةِ اتِّصَالِ نَسَبِهِ بِهِ عَلَى ثَلَاثِ طَرَائِقَ.

وَالثَّانِي: أَنَّهُ مِنْ سُلَالَةِ عَابَر، وَهُوَ هُودٌ، عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ، وَاخْتَلَفُوا فِي كَيْفِيَّةِ اتِّصَالِ نَسَبِهِ بِهِ عَلَى ثَلَاثِ طَرَائِقَ أَيْضًا.

وَالثَّالِثُ: أَنَّهُ مِنْ سُلَالَةِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْخَلِيلِ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ، وَاخْتَلَفُوا فِي كَيْفِيَّةِ اتِّصَالِ نَسَبِهِ بِهِ عَلَى ثَلَاثِ طَرَائِقَ أَيْضًا. وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ ذَلِكَ مُسْتَقْصًى الْإِمَامُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو عُمَرَ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْبَرِّ النَّمري، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، فِي كِتَابِهِ [الْمُسَمَّى] : "الْإِنْبَاهُ عَلَى ذِكْرِ أُصُولِ الْقَبَائِلِ الرُّوَاةِ" .

وَمَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ: "كَانَ رَجُلًا مِنَ الْعَرَبِ" يَعْنِي: الْعَرَبُ الْعَارِبَةُ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا قَبْلَ الْخَلِيلِ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، مِنْ سُلَالَةِ سَامِ بْنِ نُوحٍ. وَعَلَى الْقَوْلِ الثَّالِثِ: كَانَ مِنْ سُلَالَةِ الْخَلِيلِ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَلَيْسَ هَذَا بِالْمَشْهُورِ عِنْدَهُمْ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ. وَلَكِنْ فِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ مرَّ بِنَفَرٍ مِنْ "أسلَمَ" يَنْتَضِلُونَ، فَقَالَ: "ارْمُوا بَنِي إِسْمَاعِيلَ، فَإِنَّ أَبَاكُمْ كَانَ رَامِيًا" . فَأَسْلَمُ قَبِيلَةٌ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ، وَالْأَنْصَارُ أَوْسُهَا وَخَزْرَجُهَا مِنْ غَسَّانَ مِنْ عَرَبِ الْيَمَنِ مِنْ سَبَأٍ، نَزَلُوا بِيَثْرِبَ لَمَّا تَفَرَّقَتْ سَبَأٌ فِي الْبِلَادِ، حِينَ بَعَثَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ سَيْلَ الْعَرِمِ، وَنَزَلَتْ طَائِفَةٌ مِنْهُمْ بِالشَّامِ، وَإِنَّمَا قِيلَ لَهُمْ: غَسَّان بِمَاءٍ نَزَلُوا عَلَيْهِ قيلَ: بِالْيَمَنِ. وَقِيلَ: إِنَّهُ قَرِيبٌ مِنَ المُشَلَّل ، كَمَا قَالَ حَسَّانُ بْنُ ثَابِتٍ:

إمَّا سَألت فَإنَّا مَعْشَرٌ نُجُبٌ ... الأزْدُ نِسْبَتُنَا، وَالْمَاءُ غَسَّانُ 

وَمَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ: "وُلِدَ لَهُ عَشَرَةٌ مِنَ الْعَرَبِ" أَيْ: كَانَ مِنْ نسله هؤلاء العشرة الذين يرجع إِلَيْهِمْ أُصُولُ الْقَبَائِلِ مِنْ عَرَبِ الْيَمَنِ، لَا أَنَّهُمْ وُلِدُوا مِنْ صُلْبِهِ، بَلْ مِنْهُمْ مَنْ بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَهُ الْأَبَوَانِ وَالثَّلَاثَةُ وَالْأَقَلُّ وَالْأَكْثَرُ، كَمَا هُوَ مُقَرَّرٌ مُبِينٌ فِي مَوَاضِعِهِ مِنْ كُتِبِ النَّسَبِ.

وَمَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ: "فَتَيَامَنَ مِنْهُمْ سِتَّةٌ، وَتَشَاءَمَ مِنْهُمْ أَرْبَعَةٌ" أَيْ: بَعْدَ مَا أَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ سَيْلَ الْعَرِمِ، مِنْهُمْ مَنْ أَقَامَ بِبِلَادِهِمْ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ نَزَحَ عَنْهَا إِلَى غَيْرِهَا، وَكَانَ مِنْ أَمْرِ السَّدِّ أَنَّهُ كَانَ الْمَاءُ يَأْتِيهِمْ مِنْ بَيْنِ جَبَلَيْنِ وَتَجْتَمِعُ إِلَيْهِ أَيْضًا سُيُولُ أَمَطَارِهِمْ وَأَوْدِيَتِهِمْ، فعَمَدَ مُلُوكُهُمُ الْأَقَادِمُ، فَبَنَوْا بَيْنَهُمَا سَدًا عَظِيمًا مُحْكَمًا حَتَّى ارْتَفَعَ الْمَاءُ، وحُكمَ عَلَى حَافَاتِ ذَيْنَكِ الْجَبَلَيْنِ، فَغَرَسُوا الْأَشْجَارَ وَاسْتَغَلُّوا الثِّمَارَ فِي غَايَةِ مَا يَكُونُ مِنَ الْكَثْرَةِ وَالْحُسْنِ، كَمَا ذَكَرَ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ، مِنْهُمْ قَتَادَةُ: أَنَّ الْمَرْأَةَ كَانَتْ تَمْشِي تَحْتَ الْأَشْجَارِ وَعَلَى رَأْسِهَا مِكْتَلٌ أَوْ زِنْبِيلٌ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي تُخْتَرَفُ فِيهِ الثِّمَارُ، فَيَتَسَاقَطُ مِنَ الْأَشْجَارِ فِي ذَلِكَ مَا يَمْلَؤُهُ مِنْ غَيْرِ أَنَّ يَحْتَاجَ إِلَى كُلْفَةٍ وَلَا قُطَّاف، لِكَثْرَتِهِ وَنُضْجِهِ وَاسْتِوَائِهِ، وَكَانَ هَذَا السَّدُّ بِمَأْرَبَ: بَلْدَةٌ بَيْنَهَا وَبَيْنَ صَنْعَاءَ ثَلَاثُ مَرَاحِلَ، وَيُعْرَفُ بِسَدِّ مَأْرَبَ.

وَذَكَرَ آخَرُونَ أَنَّهُ لَمْ يَكُنْ بِبَلَدِهِمْ شَيْءٌ مِنَ الذُّبَابِ وَلَا الْبَعُوضِ وَلَا الْبَرَاغِيثِ، وَلَا شَيْءٌ مِنَ الْهَوَامِّ، وَذَلِكَ لِاعْتِدَالِ الْهَوَاءِ وَصِحَّةِ الْمِزَاجِ وَعِنَايَةِ اللَّهِ بِهِمْ، لِيُوَحِّدُوهُ وَيَعْبُدُوهُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَقَدْ كَانَ لِسَبَإٍ فِي مَسْكَنِهِمْ آيَةٌ﴾ ، ثُمَّ فَسَّرَهَا بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿جَنَّتَانِ عَنْ يَمِينٍ وَشِمَالٍ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ نَاحِيَتَيِ الْجَبَلَيْنِ وَالْبَلْدَةُ بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ، ﴿كُلُوا مِنْ رِزْقِ رَبِّكُمْ وَاشْكُرُوا لَهُ بَلْدَةٌ طَيِّبَةٌ وَرَبٌّ غَفُورٌ﴾ أَيْ: غَفُورٌ لَكُمْ إِنِ اسْتَمْرَرْتُمْ عَلَى التَّوْحِيدِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَعْرَضُوا﴾ أَيْ: عَنْ تَوْحِيدِ اللَّهِ وَعِبَادَتِهِ وَشُكْرِهِ عَلَى مَا أَنْعَمَ بِهِ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَعَدَلُوا إِلَى عِبَادَةِ الشَّمْسِ، كَمَا قَالَ هُدْهُدُ سُلَيْمَانَ: ﴿وَجِئْتُكَ مِنْ سَبَإٍ بِنَبَإٍ يَقِينٍ. إِنِّي وَجَدْتُ امْرَأَةً تَمْلِكُهُمْ وَأُوتِيَتْ مِنْ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ وَلَهَا عَرْشٌ عَظِيمٌ. وَجَدْتُهَا وَقَوْمَهَا يَسْجُدُونَ لِلشَّمْسِ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ وَزَيَّنَ لَهُمُ الشَّيْطَانُ أَعْمَالَهُمْ فَصَدَّهُمْ عَنِ السَّبِيلِ فَهُمْ لَا يَهْتَدُونَ﴾ [النَّمْلِ: ٢٢، ٢٤] .

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ وَهْبِ بْنِ مُنَبّه: بَعَثَ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِمْ ثَلَاثَةَ عَشَرَ نَبِيًّا.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّي: أَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِمُ اثْنَيْ عَشَرَ أَلْفَ نَبِيٍّ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَأَرْسَلْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ سَيْلَ الْعَرِمِ﴾ : قِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ بِالْعَرِمِ الْمِيَاهُ. وَقِيلَ: الْوَادِي. وَقِيلَ: الجُرَذ. وَقِيلَ: الْمَاءُ الْغَزِيرُ. فَيَكُونُ مِنْ بَابِ إِضَافَةِ الِاسْمِ إِلَى صِفَتِهِ، مِثْلَ: "مَسْجِدُ الْجَامِعِ". وَ"سَعِيدُ كُرْز" حَكَى ذَلِكَ السُّهَيْلِيُّ. 

وَذَكَرَ غَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنْهُمُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَوَهْبُ بْنُ مُنَبِّهٍ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ؛ أَنَّ اللَّهَ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، لَمَّا أَرَادَ عُقُوبَتَهُمْ بِإِرْسَالِ الْعَرِمِ عَلَيْهِمْ، بَعَثَ عَلَى السَّدِّ دَابَّةً مِنَ الْأَرْضِ، يُقَالُ لَهَا: "الجُرَذ" نَقَبَتْهُ -قَالَ وَهْبُ بْنُ مُنَبِّهٍ: وَقَدْ كَانُوا يَجِدُونَ فِي كُتُبِهِمْ أَنَّ سَبَبَ خَرَابِ هَذَا السَّدِّ هُوَ الجُرَذ فَكَانُوا يَرْصُدُونَ عِنْدَهُ السَّنَانِيرَ بُرْهَةً مِنَ الزَّمَانِ، فَلَمَّا جَاءَ الْقَدَرُ غَلَبَتِ الْفَأْرُ السَّنَانِيرَ، وَوَلَجَتْ إِلَى السَّدّ فَنَقَبَتْهُ، فَانْهَارَ عَلَيْهِمْ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ وَغَيْرُهُ: الجُرَذ: هُوَ الخَلْد، نَقَبَتْ أَسَافِلَهُ حَتَّى إِذَا ضَعف ووَهَى، وَجَاءَتْ أَيَّامُ السُّيُولِ، صَدمَ الماءُ البناءَ فَسَقَطَ، فَانْسَابَ الْمَاءُ فِي أَسْفَلِ الْوَادِي، وخرّبَ مَا بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ مِنَ الْأَبْنِيَةِ وَالْأَشْجَارِ وَغَيْرِ ذَلِكَ، وَنَضَبَ الْمَاءُ عَنِ الْأَشْجَارِ الَّتِي فِي الْجَبَلَيْنِ عَنْ يَمِينٍ وَشِمَالٍ، فَيَبِسَتْ وَتَحَطَّمَتْ، وَتَبَدَّلَتْ تِلْكَ الْأَشْجَارُ الْمُثْمِرَةُ الْأَنِيقَةُ النَّضِرَةُ، كَمَا قَالَ اللَّهُ وَتَعَالَى: ﴿وَبَدَّلْنَاهُمْ بِجَنَّتَيْهِمْ جَنَّتَيْنِ ذَوَاتَيْ أُكُلٍ خَمْطٍ﴾ .

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وعِكْرِمة، وَعَطَاءٌ الخُرَاساني، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، والسُّدِّي: وَهُوَ الْأَرَاكُ، وَأَكْلَةُ البَرير.

﴿وَأَثْل﴾ : قَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: هُوَ الطَّرْفاء.

وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُ: هُوَ شَجَرٌ يُشْبِهُ الطَّرْفَاءَ. وَقِيلَ: هُوَ السّمُر. فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَشَيْءٍ مِنْ سِدْرٍ قَلِيلٍ﴾ : لَمَّا كَانَ أجودَ هَذِهِ الْأَشْجَارِ الْمُبْدَلِ بِهَا هُوَ السّدْر قَالَ: ﴿وَشَيْءٍ مِنْ سِدْرٍ قَلِيلٍ﴾ ، فَهَذَا الَّذِي صَارَ أَمْرُ تَيْنك الْجَنَّتَيْنِ إِلَيْهِ، بَعْدَ الثِّمَارِ النَّضِيجَةِ وَالْمَنَاظِرِ الْحَسَنَةِ، وَالظِّلَالِ الْعَمِيقَةِ وَالْأَنْهَارِ الْجَارِيَةِ، تَبَدَّلَتْ إِلَى شَجَرِ الْأَرَاكِ وَالطَّرْفَاءِ والسّدْر ذِي الشَّوْكِ الْكَثِيرِ وَالثَّمَرِ الْقَلِيلِ. وَذَلِكَ بِسَبَبِ كُفْرِهِمْ وَشِرْكِهِمْ بِاللَّهِ، وَتَكْذِيبِهِمُ الْحَقَّ وَعُدُولِهِمْ عَنْهُ إِلَى الْبَاطِلِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿ذَلِكَ جَزَيْنَاهُمْ بِمَا كَفَرُوا وَهَلْ نُجَازِي إِلا الْكَفُورَ﴾ أَيْ: عَاقَبْنَاهُمْ بِكُفْرِهِمْ.

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: وَلَا يُعَاقَبُ إِلَّا الْكُفُورُ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: صَدَقَ اللَّهُ الْعَظِيمُ. لَا يُعَاقَبُ بِمِثْلِ فِعْلِهِ إِلَّا الْكُفُورُ. وَقَالَ طَاوُسٌ: لَا يُنَاقَشُ إِلَّا الْكُفُورُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الحسين، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عُمَرَ بْنُ النَّحَّاسِ الرَّمْلِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا حَجَّاجُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو الْبَيْدَاءِ، عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ صَالِحٍ التَّغْلِبِيِّ ، عَنِ ابْنِ خِيرَةَ -وَكَانَ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ-قَالَ: جَزَاءُ الْمَعْصِيَةِ الْوَهْنُ فِي الْعِبَادَةِ، وَالضِّيقُ فِي الْمَعِيشَةِ، وَالتَّعَسُّرُ فِي اللَّذَّةِ. قِيلَ: وَمَا التَّعَسُّرُ فِي اللَّذَّةِ؟ قَالَ: لَا يُصَادِفُ لَذَّةً حَلَالًا إِلَّا جَاءَهُ مَنْ يُنَغِّصه إِيَّاهَا.

---

## 34:18-19 — verses 18-19 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted, mentions the state of well-being and blessing they were in, the pleasant and abundant life, the flourishing lands, the secure dwellings, and the connected, closely-spaced villages, one adjoining the other, with abundant trees, crops, and fruits, such that their traveler had no need to carry provisions or water. Rather, wherever he stopped he would find water and fruit, resting at midday in one village and spending the night in another, according to what they needed for their journey. Therefore He, exalted, said: {And We placed between them and the towns which We had blessed}. Wahb ibn Munabbih said: these are villages in Sana'a. Abu Malik said the same.

Mujahid, al-Hasan, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Malik (narrating from Zayd ibn Aslam), Qatadah, al-Dahhak, al-Suddi, Ibn Zayd, and others said: it means the villages of Syria (al-Sham). What they mean is that they used to travel from Yemen to Syria through visible, connected villages.

Al-'Awfi reported from Ibn 'Abbas: "the towns which We had blessed" means Bayt al-Maqdis (Jerusalem).

Al-'Awfi also reported from him: they are Arab villages between Medina and Syria.

{Visible towns} means clear and evident, known to travelers, who would rest at midday in one and spend the night in another. Therefore He said: {And We had determined the journey therein}, meaning: We made them proportionate to what travelers needed. {Travel therein by nights and days, secure}, meaning: security was assured for them in their travel by night and by day.

{But they said: "Our Lord, make the distance between our journeys longer," and they wronged themselves}. Others read it as "ba'id bayna asfarina" (make distant between our journeys). This was because they grew arrogant with this blessing, as Ibn 'Abbas, Mujahid, al-Hasan, and others stated, and they came to prefer wastelands and desolate expanses which required provisions, mounts, and travel through scorching heat and dangers to cross. This is similar to when the Children of Israel asked Musa (peace be upon him) that Allah bring forth for them from what the earth grows, its herbs, cucumbers, garlic, lentils, and onions, even though they were in a pleasant life with manna and quails and whatever food, drink, and fine clothing they desired. Therefore He said to them: {Would you exchange what is lower for what is better? Go down to a city, for you shall have what you have asked for. And they were struck with humiliation and wretchedness and returned with wrath from Allah} [al-Baqarah: 61]. And He, exalted, said: {And how many a town have We destroyed that was insolent in its manner of living} [al-Qasas: 58]. And He, exalted, said: {And Allah presents an example: a city which was safe and secure, its provision coming to it in abundance from every location, but it denied the favors of Allah, so Allah made it taste the garment of hunger and fear for what they had been doing} [al-Nahl: 112]. And He said regarding these people: {and they wronged themselves}, that is, through their disbelief, {so We made them narrations and We tore them apart into fragments}, meaning: We made them a topic of talk among people, a tale told in evening gatherings about their news, and how Allah plotted against them, and scattered their unity after it had been gathered together in harmony and pleasant living, so that they were dispersed in the lands, here and there. This is why the Arabs say of a people when they have scattered: "they scattered like the hands of Saba'" and "the hands of Saba'," and "they scattered utterly asunder."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] I heard 'Ikrimah relating the account of the people of Saba'. He said: {There was certainly a sign for Saba' in their dwelling place: two gardens, on the right and on the left} up to His saying: {So We sent upon them the flood of al-'Arim}. There were soothsayers (kahins) among them, and the devils would eavesdrop and steal reports, informing the soothsayers of some news of heaven. Among them was a soothsayer, a nobleman of great wealth, and he was informed that the end of their affair had drawn near, and that punishment had come to overshadow them. He did not know what to do, for he had much wealth in property. So he said to one of his sons, the one most honored through his maternal relatives: "Tomorrow, when I command you to do something, do not do it. When I rebuke you, rebuke me back. When I strike at you, slap me." The son said: "O my father, do not do this, this is a grave and difficult matter." He said: "O my son, a matter has occurred which must be." He kept at it until the son agreed to it.

When morning came and the people had gathered, he said: "O my son, do such and such." The son refused, so his father rebuked him, and the son answered back. This continued between them until the father struck at him, whereupon the son leapt upon his father and slapped him. The father said: "My son slaps me? Bring me the knife!" They said: "What will you do with the knife?" He said: "I will slaughter him." They said: "Would you slaughter your own son? Slap him or do whatever else you wish." He refused. So they sent to the boy's maternal relatives and informed them of this. His maternal uncles came and said: "Take from us whatever compensation you wish." He refused, insisting on slaughtering him. They said: "Then you will die before you slaughter him." He said: "If matters have come to this, then I see no reason to remain in a land where I am kept from my own child. Buy my houses from me, buy my land from me." He persisted until he had sold his houses, his land, and his property. When the price was in his hand and secured, he said: "O my people, punishment has come to overshadow you, and the end of your affair has drawn near. So whoever among you wants a new home, a strong camel, and a distant journey, let him join 'Amman. And whoever among you wants wine, leavened bread, and fresh juice," and a word which Ibrahim said he did not remember, "let him join Busra. And whoever wants the deep-rooted ones in the mud, those who feed in times of drought, those who dwell in the shallows, let him join Yathrib, the place of palm trees."

His people obeyed him. The people of 'Uman went out to 'Uman. Ghassan went out to Busra. Al-Aws, al-Khazraj, and Banu 'Uthman went out to Yathrib, the place of palm trees. They came upon Batn Marr, and Banu 'Uthman said: "This is a good place, we do not seek any substitute for it." So they settled there, and were named Khuza'ah for this reason, because they separated from their companions. Al-Aws and al-Khazraj continued on until they settled in Medina. The people of 'Uman proceeded to 'Uman, and Ghassan proceeded to Busra.

This is a gharib (rare), remarkable athar (report). This soothsayer was 'Amr ibn 'Amir, one of the chiefs of Yemen, one of the great men of Saba' and their soothsayers.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq ibn Yasar mentioned at the beginning of the Sirah the account of 'Amr ibn 'Amir, who was the first to leave the lands of Yemen because he sensed the coming of the flood of al-'Arim. He said: the cause of 'Amr ibn 'Amir's departure from Yemen, as related to me by Abu Zayd al-Ansari, was that he saw a rat digging in the dam of Ma'rib, which held back water from them so that they could direct it wherever they wished in their land. He realized that the dam could not endure under such conditions, so he resolved to move away from Yemen, and he devised a scheme regarding his people. He commanded his youngest son that if he spoke harshly to him and struck him, the son should get up and slap him back. The son did as he was commanded, and 'Amr said: "I will not remain in a land where my youngest child has slapped my face." He then offered his wealth for sale, and some of the nobles of Yemen said: "Take advantage of 'Amr's anger." So they bought his wealth from him, and he moved away with his children and grandchildren. The tribe of Azd said: "We will not stay behind 'Amr ibn 'Amir." So they sold their wealth and departed with him. They traveled until they settled in the lands of 'Akk, passing through while seeking out lands to settle. 'Akk fought them, and the fighting went back and forth between them. Concerning this, 'Abbas ibn Mirdas al-Sulami said:

"And 'Akk, son of 'Adnan, those who overcame Ghassan, until they were driven off time after time."

This verse is from a longer poem of his.

He said: then they departed from them and dispersed into the lands. The family of Jafnah ibn 'Amr ibn 'Amir settled in Syria. Al-Aws and al-Khazraj settled in Yathrib. Khuza'ah settled at Marr. The Azd of al-Sarah settled in al-Sarah. The Azd of 'Uman settled in 'Uman. Then Allah sent the flood upon the dam and it collapsed, and it was concerning this that Allah, mighty and exalted, revealed these verses.

Al-Suddi mentioned the story of 'Amr ibn 'Amir similarly to what Muhammad ibn Ishaq mentioned, except that he said "so he commanded his brother's son" instead of "his son," up to his saying: "so he sold his property and departed with his family, and they dispersed." Ibn Abi Hatim narrated it.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Ibn Ishaq said: they claim that 'Amr ibn 'Amir, who was the uncle of the people, was a soothsayer, and he perceived through his soothsaying that his people would be torn apart and that the distances between their journeys would be lengthened. So he said to them: "I know that you will be torn apart, so whoever among you has a distant ambition, a strong camel, and new water-skins, let him join Kas or Karud." He said: thus was the tribe of Wadi'ah ibn 'Amr formed.

"Whoever among you has a rising ambition and an abandoned matter, let him join the land of Shan." So it was Awf ibn Amr, and they are the ones called Bariq. "And whoever among you desires an immediate life and a secure sanctuary, let him join the two Arzin." So it was Khuza'ah. "And whoever among you desires the firmly rooted ones in the mud, the ones who provide food in drought, let him join Yathrib, the place of palm trees." So it was al-Aws and al-Khazraj, these being the two tribes of the Ansar. "And whoever among you desires wine and bread, gold and silk, kingship and command, let him join Kutha and Busra." So it was Ghassan, the Banu Jafnah, kings of Syria. "And whoever among them was in Iraq..."

Ibn Ishaq said: I heard some of the people of knowledge say that it was Tarifah, the wife of Amr ibn Amir, who said this statement. She was a soothsayer, and she saw this in her soothsaying. God knows best which of these accounts is correct.

Sa'id said, from Qatadah, from al-Sha'bi: as for Ghassan, they joined Syria; as for the Ansar, they joined Yathrib; as for Khuza'ah, they joined Tihamah; as for al-Azd, they joined Oman. So God scattered them, every scattering. Narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim and Ibn Jarir.

Then Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: Abu Ubaydah narrated to me, saying: al-A'sha, that is, the A'sha of Banu Qays ibn Tha'labah, whose name was Maymun ibn Qays, said:

"In that there is an example for one who takes heed, and Ma'rib, which the flood-dam destroyed..."

"Marble which Himyar built for them, so that when its channel came, it did not cease..."

"It watered the crops and their vines, abundantly, their water being apportioned..."

"So they became scattered, unable to obtain from it even the drink of a weaned infant."

Regarding the statement of the Exalted: {Indeed in that are signs for every one who is greatly patient and greatly thankful}, that is: in what befell these people of retribution and punishment, of the change of blessing and the turning away of well-being, as a punishment for what they committed of disbelief and sins, there is a lesson and a proof for every servant who is greatly patient over calamities and greatly thankful for blessings.

Imam Ahmad said: Abd al-Rahman and Abd al-Razzaq al-Ma'ni narrated to us, both saying: Sufyan informed us, from Abu Ishaq, from al-Ayzar ibn Hurayth, from Umar ibn Sa'd, from his father, that is, Sa'd ibn Abi Waqqas, may God be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "I am amazed at God's decree for the believer. If good befalls him, he praises his Lord and gives thanks; and if a calamity befalls him, he praises his Lord and is patient. The believer is rewarded in everything, even in the morsel he raises to his wife's mouth."

Al-Nasa'i narrated it in "al-Yawm wa'l-Laylah," from the hadith of Abu Ishaq al-Sabi'i, with this chain, and it is a gharib (singular) hadith, from the narration of Umar ibn Sa'd, from his father. However, it has a corroborating witness in the two Sahihs, from the hadith of Abu Hurayrah: "It is amazing for the believer, God does not decree any decree for him except that it is good for him. If ease befalls him, he is thankful, and that is good for him; and if hardship befalls him, he is patient, and that is good for him. And that applies to no one except the believer."

Abd said: Yunus narrated to us, from Shayban, from Qatadah, regarding {Indeed in that are signs for every one who is greatly patient and greatly thankful}, he said: Mutarrif used to say: What an excellent servant is the one who is greatly patient and greatly thankful, who gives thanks when given, and is patient when tried.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَذْكُرُ تَعَالَى مَا كَانُوا فِيهِ مِنَ الغِبْطة وَالنِّعْمَةِ، وَالْعَيْشِ الْهَنِيِّ الرَّغِيدِ، وَالْبِلَادِ الرَّخِيَّةِ، وَالْأَمَاكِنِ الْآمِنَةِ، وَالْقُرَى الْمُتَوَاصِلَةِ الْمُتَقَارِبَةِ، بَعْضِهَا مِنْ بَعْضٍ، مع كثرة أشجارها وزروعها وثمارها، بحيث إِنَّ مُسَافِرَهُمْ لَا يَحْتَاجُ إِلَى حَمل زَادٍ وَلَا مَاءٍ، بَلْ حَيْثُ نَزَلَ وَجَدَ مَاءً وَثَمَرًا، ويَقيل فِي قَرْيَةٍ وَيَبِيتُ فِي أُخْرَى، بِمِقْدَارِ مَا يَحْتَاجُونَ إِلَيْهِ فِي سَيْرِهِمْ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَجَعَلْنَا بَيْنَهُمْ وَبَيْنَ الْقُرَى الَّتِي بَارَكْنَا فِيهَا﴾ ، قَالَ وَهْبُ بْنُ مُنَبِّهٍ: هِيَ قُرًى بِصَنْعَاءَ. وَكَذَا قَالَ أَبُو مَالِكٍ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وَمَالِكٌ عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَقَتَادَةَ، وَالضَّحَّاكِ، والسُّدِّي، وَابْنِ زَيْدٍ وَغَيْرِهِمْ : يَعْنِي: قُرَى الشَّامِ. يَعْنُونَ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا يَسِيرُونَ مِنَ الْيَمَنِ إِلَى الشَّامِ فِي قُرًى ظَاهِرَةٍ مُتَوَاصِلَةٍ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: الْقُرَى الَّتِي بَارَكْنَا فِيهَا : بَيْتُ الْمَقْدِسِ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنْهُ أَيْضًا: هِيَ قُرًى عَرَبِيَّةٌ بَيْنَ الْمَدِينَةِ وَالشَّامِ.

﴿قُرًى ظَاهِرَةً﴾ أَيْ: بَيِّنَةً وَاضِحَةً، يَعْرِفُهَا الْمُسَافِرُونَ، يَقيلون فِي وَاحِدَةٍ، وَيَبِيتُونَ فِي أُخْرَى؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَقَدَّرْنَا فِيهَا السَّيْرَ﴾ أَيْ: جَعَلْنَاهَا بِحَسْبَ مَا يَحْتَاجُ الْمُسَافِرُونَ إِلَيْهِ، ﴿سِيرُوا فِيهَا لَيَالِيَ وَأَيَّامًا آمِنِينَ﴾ أَيِ: الْأَمْنُ حَاصِلٌ لَهُمْ فِي سَيْرِهِمْ لَيْلًا وَنَهَارًا.

﴿فَقَالُوا رَبَّنَا بَاعِدْ بَيْنَ أَسْفَارِنَا وَظَلَمُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ﴾ ، وَقَرَأَ آخَرُونَ: "بَعِّدْ بَيْنِ أَسْفَارِنَا "، وَذَلِكَ أَنَّهُمْ بَطروا هَذِهِ النِّعْمَةَ -كَمَا قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٌ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ-وَأَحَبُّوا مَفَاوِزَ وَمَهَامِهَ يَحْتَاجُونَ فِي قَطْعِهَا إِلَى الزَّادِ وَالرَّوَاحِلِ وَالسَّيْرِ فِي الحَرُور وَالْمَخَاوِفِ، كَمَا طَلَبَ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ مِنْ مُوسَى أَنْ يُخْرِجَ اللَّهُ لَهُمْ مِمَّا تُنْبِتُ الْأَرْضُ، مِنْ بَقْلِهَا وَقِثَّائِهَا وَفُومِهَا وَعَدَسِهَا وَبَصَلِهَا، مَعَ أَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا فِي عَيْشٍ رَغِيدٍ فِي مَنّ وَسَلْوَى وَمَا يَشْتَهُونَ مِنْ مَآكِلَ وَمَشَارِبَ وَمَلَابِسَ مُرْتَفِعَةٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ لَهُمْ: ﴿أَتَسْتَبْدِلُونَ الَّذِي هُوَ أَدْنَى بِالَّذِي هُوَ خَيْرٌ اهْبِطُوا مِصْرًا فَإِنَّ لَكُمْ مَا سَأَلْتُمْ وَضُرِبَتْ عَلَيْهِمُ الذِّلَّةُ وَالْمَسْكَنَةُ وَبَاءُوا بِغَضَبٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٦١] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَكَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا مِنْ قَرْيَةٍ بَطِرَتْ مَعِيشَتَهَا﴾ [الْقَصَصِ: ٥٨] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَضَرَبَ اللَّهُ مَثَلا قَرْيَةً كَانَتْ آمِنَةً مُطْمَئِنَّةً يَأْتِيهَا رِزْقُهَا رَغَدًا مِنْ كُلِّ مَكَانٍ فَكَفَرَتْ بِأَنْعُمِ اللَّهِ فَأَذَاقَهَا اللَّهُ لِبَاسَ الْجُوعِ وَالْخَوْفِ بِمَا كَانُوا يَصْنَعُونَ﴾ [النَّحْلِ: ١١٢] . وَقَالَ فِي حَقِّ هَؤُلَاءِ: ﴿وَظَلَمُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: بِكُفْرِهِمْ، ﴿فَجَعَلْنَاهُمْ أَحَادِيثَ وَمَزَّقْنَاهُمْ كُلَّ مُمَزَّقٍ﴾ أَيْ: جَعَلْنَاهُمْ حَدِيثًا لِلنَّاسِ، وَسمَرًا يَتَحَدَّثُونَ بِهِ مِنْ خَبَرِهِمْ، وَكَيْفَ مَكَرَ اللَّهُ بِهِمْ، وَفَرَّقَ شَمْلَهُمْ بَعْدَ الِاجْتِمَاعِ وَالْأُلْفَةِ وَالْعَيْشِ الْهَنِيءِ تَفَرَّقُوا فِي الْبِلَادِ هَاهُنَا وَهَاهُنَا؛ وَلِهَذَا تَقُولُ الْعَرَبُ فِي الْقَوْمِ إِذَا تَفَرَّقُوا: "تَفَرَّقُوا أَيْدِيَ سَبَأٍ" "وَأَيَادِيَ سَبَأٍ" وَ "تَفَرَّقُوا شَذَرَ مَذَرَ". 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سَعِيدٍ بْنُ يَحْيَى بْنِ سَعِيدٍ الْقَطَّانُ، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ حَبِيبِ بْنِ الشَّهِيدِ، سَمِعْتُ أَبِي يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ عِكْرِمَةَ يُحَدِّثُ بِحَدِيثِ أَهْلِ سَبَأٍ، قَالَ: ﴿لَقَدْ كَانَ لِسَبَإٍ فِي مَسْكَنِهِمْ آيَةٌ جَنَّتَانِ [عَنْ يَمِينٍ وَشِمَالٍ] ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَأَرْسَلْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ سَيْلَ الْعَرِمِ﴾ وكانت فيهم كَهَنَةٌ، وَكَانَتِ الشَّيَاطِينُ يَسْتَرِقُونَ السَّمْعَ، فَأَخْبَرُوا الْكَهَنَةَ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْ أَخْبَارِ السَّمَاءِ، فَكَانَ فِيهِمْ رَجُلٌ كَاهِنٌ شَرِيفٌ كَثِيرُ الْمَالِ، وَإِنَّهُ خُبّر أَنَّ زَوَالَ أَمْرِهِمْ قَدْ دَنَا، وَأَنَّ الْعَذَابَ قَدْ أَظَلَّهُمْ . فَلَمْ يَدْرِ كَيْفَ يَصْنَعُ؛ لِأَنَّهُ كَانَ لَهُ مَالٌ كَثِيرٌ مِنْ عَقَارٍ، فَقَالَ لِرَجُلٍ مِنْ بَنِيهِ -وَهُوَ أَعَزُّهُمْ أَخْوَالًا-: إِذَا كَانَ غَدًا وَأَمَرْتُكَ بِأَمْرٍ فَلَا تَفْعَلْ، فَإِذَا انْتَهَرْتُكَ فَانْتَهِرْنِي، فَإِذَا تَنَاوَلْتُكَ فَالْطِمْنِي. فَقَالَ: يَا أَبَتِ، لَا تَفْعَلْ، إِنَّ هَذَا أَمْرٌ عَظِيمٌ، وَأَمْرٌ شَدِيدٌ، قَالَ: يَا بُنَيَّ، قَدْ حَدَثَ أَمْرٌ لَا بُدَّ مِنْهُ. فَلَمْ يَزَلْ بِهِ حَتَّى وَافَاهُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ. فَلَمَّا أَصْبَحُوا وَاجْتَمَعَ النَّاسُ، قَالَ: يَا بُنَيَّ، افْعَلْ كَذَا وَكَذَا. فَأَبَى، فَانْتَهَرَهُ أَبُوهُ، فَأَجَابَهُ، فَلَمْ يَزَلْ ذَلِكَ بَيْنَهُمَا حَتَّى تَنَاوَلَهُ أَبُوهُ، فَوَثَبَ عَلَى أَبِيهِ فَلَطَمَهُ، فَقَالَ: ابْنِي يَلْطِمُنِي؟ عَلَيّ بِالشَّفْرَةِ. قَالُوا: وَمَا تَصْنَعُ بِالشَّفْرَةِ؟ قَالَ: أَذْبَحُهُ. قَالُوا: تَذْبَحُ ابْنَكَ. الْطِمْهُ أَوِ اصْنَعْ مَا بَدَا لَكَ. قَالَ: فَأَبَى، قَالَ: فَأَرْسَلُوا إِلَى أَخْوَالِهِ فَأَعْلَمُوهُمْ ذَلِكَ، فَجَاءَ أَخْوَالُهُ فَقَالُوا: خُذْ مِنَّا مَا بَدَا لَكَ. فَأَبَى إِلَّا أَنْ يَذْبَحَهُ. قَالُوا: فَلَتَمُوتَنَّ قَبْلَ أَنْ تَذْبَحَهُ. قَالَ: فَإِذَا كَانَ الْحَدِيثُ هَكَذَا فَإِنِّي لَا أَرَى أَنْ أُقِيمَ بِبَلَدٍ يُحَالُ بَيْنِي وَبَيْنَ وَلَدِي فِيهِ، اشْتَرُوا مِنِّي دُورِي، اشْتَرُوا مِنِّي أَرْضِي، فَلَمْ يَزَلْ حَتَّى باع دوره وأرضيه وَعَقَارَهُ، فَلَمَّا صَارَ الثَّمَنُ فِي يَدِهِ وَأَحْرَزَهُ، قَالَ: أَيْ قَوْمِ، إِنَّ الْعَذَابَ قَدْ أَظَلَّكُمْ، وَزَوَالُ أَمْرِكُمْ قَدْ دَنَا، فَمَنْ أَرَادَ مِنْكُمْ دَارًا جَدِيدًا، وَجَمَلًا شَدِيدًا، وَسَفَرًا بَعِيدًا، فَلْيَلْحَقْ بِعَمَّانَ. وَمَنْ أَرَادَ مِنْكُمُ الخَمْر والخَمير والعَصير -وَكَلِمَةً، قَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ: لَمْ أَحْفَظْهَا-فَلْيَلْحَقْ ببصْرَى، وَمَنْ أَرَادَ الرَّاسِخَاتِ فِي الْوَحْلِ، الْمُطْعِمَاتِ فِي الْمَحْلِ، الْمُقِيمَاتِ فِي الضَّحْلِ، فَلْيَلْحَقْ بِيَثْرِبَ ذَاتِ نَخْلٍ. فَأَطَاعَهُ قَوْمُهُ فَخَرَجَ أَهْلُ عُمَانَ إِلَى عُمَانَ. وَخَرَجَتْ غَسَّانُ إِلَى بُصْرَى. وَخَرَجَتِ الْأَوْسُ وَالْخَزْرَجُ وَبَنُو عُثْمَانَ إِلَى يَثْرِبَ ذَاتِ النَّخْلِ. قَالَ: فَأَتَوْا عَلَى بَطْنِ مُرٍّ فَقَالَ بَنُو عُثْمَانَ: هَذَا مَكَانٌ صَالِحٌ، لَا نَبْغِي بِهِ بَدَلًا. فَأَقَامُوا بِهِ، فَسُمُّوا لِذَلِكَ خُزَاعَةَ، لِأَنَّهُمُ انْخَزَعُوا مِنْ أَصْحَابِهِمْ، وَاسْتَقَامَتِ الْأَوْسُ وَالْخَزْرَجُ حَتَّى نَزَلُوا الْمَدِينَةَ، وَتَوَجَّهَ أَهْلُ عُمَانَ إِلَى عُمَانَ، وَتَوَجَّهَتْ غَسَّانُ إِلَى بُصْرَى.

هَذَا أَثَرٌ غَرِيبٌ عَجِيبٌ، وَهَذَا الْكَاهِنُ هُوَ عَمْرُو بْنُ عَامِرٍ أَحَدُ رُؤَسَاءِ الْيَمَنِ وَكُبَرَاءِ سَبَأٍ وَكُهَّانِهِمْ. 

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ بْنِ يَسَارٍ فِي أَوَّلِ السِّيرَةِ مَا كَانَ مِنْ أَمْرِ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَامِرٍ الَّذِي كَانَ أَوَّلَ مَنْ خَرَجَ مِنْ بِلَادِ الْيَمَنِ، بِسَبَبِ اسْتِشْعَارِهِ بِإِرْسَالِ العَرم فَقَالَ: وَكَانَ سَبَبُ خُرُوجِ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَامِرٍ مِنَ الْيَمَنِ -فِيمَا حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو زَيْدٍ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ-: أَنَّهُ رَأَى جُرَذًا يَحفر فِي سَدِّ مَأْرِبَ، الَّذِي كَانَ يَحْبِسُ عَنْهُمُ الْمَاءَ فَيَصْرِفُونَهُ حَيْثُ شاؤوا مِنْ أَرْضِهِمْ. فَعَلِمَ أَنَّهُ لَا بَقَاءَ لِلسَّدِّ عَلَى ذَلِكَ، فَاعْتَزَمَ عَلَى النَّقُلة عَنِ الْيَمَنِ فَكَادَ قَوْمَهُ، فَأَمَرَ أَصْغَرَ أَوْلَادِهِ إِذَا أَغْلَظَ لَهُ وَلَطَمَهُ أَنْ يَقُومَ إِلَيْهِ فَيَلْطِمُهُ، فَفَعَلَ ابْنُهُ مَا أَمَرَهُ بِهِ، فَقَالَ عَمْرٌو: لَا أُقِيمُ بِبَلَدٍ لَطَم وَجْهِي فِيهَا أَصْغَرُ وَلَدِي . وعرض أمواله، فقال أَشْرَافٌ مِنْ أَشْرَافِ الْيَمَنِ: اغْتَنَمُوا غَضْبَةَ عَمْرٍو. فَاشْتَرَوْا مِنْهُ أَمْوَالَهُ، وَانْتَقَلَ هُوَ فِي وَلَدِهِ وَوَلَدِ وَلَدِهِ. وَقَالَتِ الْأَزْدُ: لَا نَتَخَلَّفُ عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَامِرٍ. فَبَاعُوا أَمْوَالَهُمْ، وَخَرَجُوا مَعَهُ فَسَارُوا حَتَّى نَزَلُوا بِلَادَ "عَكَّ" مُجْتَازِينَ يَرْتَادُونَ الْبُلْدَانَ، فَحَارَبَتْهُمْ عَكُّ، وَكَانَتْ حَرْبُهُمْ سجَالا. فَفِي ذَلِكَ يَقُولُ عَبَّاسُ بْنُ مِرْدَاسَ السُّلَمِيُّ:

وَعَكَ بنُ عَدنَانَ الذين تَغَلَّبُوا ... بِغَسَّانَ، حَتَّى طُرّدُوا كُلّ مَطْرَد ...

وَهَذَا الْبَيْتُ مِنْ قَصِيدَةٍ لَهُ.

قَالَ: ثُمَّ ارْتَحَلُوا عَنْهُمْ فَتَفَرَّقُوا فِي الْبِلَادِ، فَنَزَلَ آلُ جَفْنَة بْنُ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَامِرٍ الشَّامَ، وَنَزَلَتِ الْأَوْسُ وَالْخَزْرَجُ يَثْرِبَ، وَنَزَلَتْ خُزَاعَةُ مَرّا. وَنَزَلَتْ أَزْدُ السَّرَاةِ السَّرَاةَ، وَنَزَلَتْ أَزِدُ عُمَان عُمان، ثُمَّ أَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى السَّدِّ السَّيْلَ فهدمَه، وَفِي ذَلِكَ أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَاتِ. 

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ السُّدِّيُّ قِصَّةَ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَامِرٍ بِنَحْوٍ مِمَّا ذَكَرَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، إِلَّا أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "فَأَمَرَ ابْنَ أَخِيهِ"، مَكَانَ "ابْنِهِ"، إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: "فَبَاعَ مَالَهُ وَارْتَحَلَ بِأَهْلِهِ، فَتَفَرَّقُوا". رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ حُمَيْدٍ، أَخْبَرَنَا [سَلَمَةُ] ، عَنِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ قَالَ: يَزْعُمُونَ أَنَّ عَمْرَو بْنَ عَامِرٍ -وَهُوَ عَمُّ الْقَوْمِ-كَانَ كَاهِنًا، فَرَأَى فِي كَهَانَتِهِ أَنَّ قَوْمَهُ سَيمَزّقون ويباعَدُ بَيْنَ أَسْفَارِهِمْ. فَقَالَ لَهُمْ: إِنِّي قَدْ عَلِمْتُ أَنَّكُمْ سَتُمَزَّقُونَ، فَمَنْ كَانَ مِنْكُمْ ذَا هَمٍّ بَعِيدٍ وَجَمَلٍ شَدِيدٍ، ومَزَاد جَديد -فَلْيَلْحَقْ بِكَاسٍ أَوْ كَرُودَ. قَالَ: فَكَانَتْ وَادَعَةُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو. ومَنْ كَانَ مِنْكُمْ ذَا هَمّ مُدْن، وَأَمْرٍ دَعْن، فَلْيَلْحَقْ بِأَرْضِ شَنْ. فَكَانَتْ عَوْفُ بْنُ عَمْرٍو، وَهُمُ الَّذِينَ يُقَالُ لَهُمْ: بَارِقُ. ومَنْ كَانَ مِنْكُمْ يُرِيدُ عَيْشًا آنِيًا، وَحَرَمًا آمِنًا، فَلْيَلْحَقْ بِالْأَرْزِينِ. فَكَانَتْ خُزَاعَةُ. ومَنْ كَانَ مِنْكُمْ يُرِيدُ الرَّاسِيَاتِ فِي الْوَحْلِ، الْمُطْعِمَاتِ فِي الْمَحْلِ، فَلْيَلْحَقْ بِيَثْرِبَ ذَاتِ النَّخْلِ. فَكَانَتِ الْأَوْسُ وَالْخَزْرَجُ، وَهُمَا هَذَانِ الْحَيَّانِ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ. ومَنْ كَانَ مِنْكُمْ يُرِيدُ خَمْرًا وخَميرا، وَذَهَبًا وَحَرِيرًا، وَمُلْكًا وَتَأْمِيرًا، فَلْيَلْحَقْ بكُوثي وبُصرى، فَكَانَتْ غسانَ بَنُو جَفنة ملوكُ الشَّامِ. ومَنْ كَانَ مِنْهُمْ بِالْعِرَاقِ. قَالَ ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: وَقَدْ سَمِعْتُ بَعْضَ أَهْلِ الْعِلْمِ يَقُولُ: إِنَّمَا قَالَتْ هَذِهِ الْمَقَالَةَ طريفةُ امْرَأَةُ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَامِرٍ، وَكَانَتْ كَاهِنَةً، فَرَأَتْ فِي كَهَانَتِهَا ذَلِكَ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ أَيُّ ذَلِكَ كَانَ. 

وَقَالَ سَعِيدٌ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ: أَمَّا غَسَّانُ فَلَحِقُوا بِالشَّامِ، وَأَمَّا الْأَنْصَارُ فَلَحِقُوا بِيَثْرِبَ، وَأَمَّا خُزَاعَةَ فَلَحِقُوا بِتِهَامَةَ، وَأَمَّا الْأَزْدُ فَلَحِقُوا بِعُمَانَ، فَمَزَّقَهُمُ اللَّهُ كُلَّ مُمَزَّقٍ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: حَدَّثَنِي أَبُو عُبَيْدَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ الْأَعْشَى -أَعْشَى بَنِي قَيْسِ بْنِ ثَعْلَبَةَ-وَاسْمُهُ: مَيْمُونُ بْنُ قيس: وَفي ذَاكَ للمُؤتَسي أسْوَةٌ ... ومَأربُ عَفّى عَلَيها العَرمْ ...

رُخَام بَنَتْهُ لَهُمْ حِمْيرُ ... إِذَا جاءَ مَوَارهُ لَمْ يَرمْ ...

فَأرْوَى الزُّرُوعَ وَأعنَابَها ... عَلَى سَعَة مَاؤهُمْ إذْ قُسِم ...

فَصَارُوا أيَادي مَا يَقْدرُو ... نَ منْه عَلَى شُرب طِفْل فُطِم 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَاتٍ لِكُلِّ صَبَّارٍ شَكُورٍ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ فِي هَذَا الَّذِي حَلَّ بِهَؤُلَاءِ مِنَ النِّقْمَةِ وَالْعَذَابِ، وَتَبْدِيلِ النِّعْمَةِ وَتَحْوِيلِ الْعَافِيَةِ، عقوبةَ عَلَى مَا ارْتَكَبُوهُ مِنَ الْكُفْرِ وَالْآثَامِ -لَعِبْرَةً وَدَلالةً لِكُلِّ عَبْدٍ صَبَّارٍ عَلَى الْمَصَائِبِ، شَكُورٍ عَلَى النِّعَمِ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ وَعَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ الْمَعْنِيُّ، قَالَا أَخْبَرَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ العَيْزَار بْنِ حُرَيث عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ -هُوَ سَعْدِ بْنِ أَبِي وَقَّاصٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ-قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "عَجِبْتُ مِنْ قَضَاءِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى لِلْمُؤْمِنِ، إِنْ أَصَابَهُ خَيْرٌ حَمدَ رَبَّه وَشَكَرَ، وَإِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ مُصِيبَةٌ حَمِد رَبَّهُ وصَبَر، يُؤْجَرُ الْمُؤْمِنُ فِي كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، حَتَّى فِي اللُّقْمَةِ يَرْفَعُهَا إِلَى فِي امْرَأَتِهِ".

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ فِي "الْيَوْمِ وَاللَّيْلَةَ"، مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ السَّبِيعي، بِهِ -وَهُوَ حَدِيثٌ عَزِيزٌ-مِنْ رِوَايَةِ عُمَرَ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ. وَلَكِنْ لَهُ شَاهِدٌ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ: "عَجَبًا لِلْمُؤْمِنِ لَا يَقْضِي اللَّهُ لَهُ قَضَاءً إِلَّا كَانَ خَيْرًا ، إِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ سَرَّاءُ شَكَرَ فَكَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُ، وَإِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ ضَرَّاءُ صَبَرَ فَكَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُ. وَلَيْسَ ذَلِكَ لِأَحَدٍ إِلَّا لِلْمُؤْمِنِ". 

قَالَ عَبْدٌ: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ، عَنْ شَيْبَانَ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ ﴿إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لآيَاتٍ لِكُلِّ صَبَّارٍ شَكُورٍ﴾ قَالَ: كَانَ مُطَرَّفٌ يَقُولُ: نِعْمَ الْعَبْدُ الصَّبَّارُ الشَّكُورُ، الَّذِي إِذَا أُعْطِيَ شَكَرَ، وَإِذَا ابْتُلِيَ صَبَرَ.

---

## 34:20-21 — verses 20-21 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When [Allah] the Exalted mentioned the story of Saba and what befell them in their following of desire and Satan, He told about them and about others like them who followed Iblis and desire, and opposed right guidance and true direction. He said: {And indeed Iblis's assumption about them proved true}.

Ibn Abbas and others said: this verse is like His statement, the Exalted, informing about Iblis when he refused to prostrate to Adam, then said: {Do you see this one whom You have honored above me? If You delay me until the Day of Resurrection, I will surely entice his descendants, except a few} [al-Isra: 62], then said: {Then I will surely come to them from before them and from behind them and from their right and from their left, and You will not find most of them grateful} [al-A'raf: 17]. The verses on this subject are numerous.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: When Allah sent Adam down from the Garden, with Hawwa' accompanying him, Iblis descended rejoicing over what he had gained from the two of them, and said: "If I have gained from the two parents what I have gained, then their descendants will be weaker and weaker still." That was merely an assumption on the part of Iblis, so Allah, Mighty and Majestic, revealed: {And indeed Iblis's assumption about them proved true, so they followed him, except a group of the believers}. At that, Iblis said: "I will not part from the son of Adam as long as breath remains in him. I will promise him, and give him false hopes, and deceive him." Allah then said: "By My might, I will not withhold repentance from him as long as he has not reached the death rattle, and he will not call upon Me without My answering him, nor ask of Me without My giving him, nor seek My forgiveness without My forgiving him." Reported by Ibn Abi Hatim.

Regarding His statement: {and he had no authority over them}, Ibn Abbas said: meaning, no proof.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: By Allah, he did not strike them with a staff, nor compel them to anything by force. It was nothing but delusion and false hopes that he called them to, and they answered him.

Regarding His statement: {except that We might know who believes in the Hereafter from who is in doubt concerning it}, meaning: We only gave him power over them so that the condition of whoever believes in the Hereafter, its establishment, the reckoning within it, and the requital, might become manifest, so that such a person would worship his Lord, Mighty and Majestic, well in this world, as distinguished from whoever is in doubt about it.

Regarding His statement: {and your Lord is a watchful guardian over all things}, meaning: despite His guarding, whoever went astray among those who followed Iblis did go astray, and by His guarding and safekeeping, whoever among the believers, the followers of the messengers, was kept safe, was indeed kept safe.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى قِصَّةَ سَبَأٍ وَمَا كَانَ مِنْ أَمْرِهِمْ فِي اتِّبَاعِهِمُ الْهَوَى وَالشَّيْطَانِ، أَخْبَرَ عَنْهُمْ وَعَنْ أَمْثَالِهِمْ مِمَّنِ اتَّبَعَ إِبْلِيسَ وَالْهَوَى، وَخَالَفَ الرَّشَادَ وَالْهُدَى، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ صَدَّقَ عَلَيْهِمْ إِبْلِيسُ ظَنَّهُ﴾ .

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ وَغَيْرُهُ: هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى إِخْبَارًا عَنْ إِبْلِيسٍ حِينَ امْتَنَعَ مِنَ السُّجُودِ لِآدَمَ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿أَرَأَيْتَكَ هَذَا الَّذِي كَرَّمْتَ عَلَيَّ لَئِنْ أَخَّرْتَنِ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ لأحْتَنِكَنَّ ذُرِّيَّتَهُ إِلا قَلِيلا﴾ [الْإِسْرَاءِ: ٦٢] ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿ثُمَّ لآتِيَنَّهُمْ مِنْ بَيْنِ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِمْ وَعَنْ أَيْمَانِهِمْ وَعَنْ شَمَائِلِهِمْ وَلا تَجِدُ أَكْثَرَهُمْ شَاكِرِينَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافُ: ١٧] وَالْآيَاتُ فِي هَذَا كَثِيرَةٌ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: لَمَّا أَهْبَطَ اللَّهُ آدَمَ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَمَعَهُ حَوَّاءُ، هَبَطَ إِبْلِيسُ فَرحا بِمَا أَصَابَ مِنْهُمَا، وَقَالَ: إِذَا أَصَبْتُ مِنَ الْأَبَوَيْنِ مَا أَصَبْتُ، فَالذُّرِّيَّةُ أَضْعَفُ وَأَضْعَفُ. وَكَانَ ذَلِكَ ظَنًّا مِنْ إِبْلِيسَ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَلَقَدْ صَدَّقَ عَلَيْهِمْ إِبْلِيسُ ظَنَّهُ فَاتَّبَعُوهُ إِلا فَرِيقًا مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ فَقَالَ عِنْدَ ذَلِكَ إِبْلِيسُ: "لَا أُفَارِقُ ابْنَ آدَمَ مَا دَامَ فِيهِ الرُّوحُ، أعدُه وأُمَنّيه وَأَخْدَعُهُ". فَقَالَ اللَّهُ: "وَعِزَّتِي لَا أَحْجُبُ عَنْهُ التَّوْبَةَ مَا لَمْ يُغَرغِر بِالْمَوْتِ، وَلَا يَدْعُونِي إِلَّا أَجَبْتُهُ، وَلَا يَسْأَلُنِي إِلَّا أَعْطَيْتُهُ، وَلَا يَسْتَغْفِرُنِي إِلَّا غَفَرْتُ لَهُ". رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ لَهُ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ سُلْطَانٍ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: أَيْ مِنْ حُجَّةٍ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: وَاللَّهِ مَا ضَرَبَهُمْ بِعَصَا، وَلَا أَكْرَهَهُمْ عَلَى شَيْءٍ، وَمَا كَانَ إِلَّا غُرُورًا وَأَمَانِيَّ دَعَاهُمْ إِلَيْهَا فَأَجَابُوهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِلا لِنَعْلَمَ مَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِالآخِرَةِ مِمَّنْ هُوَ مِنْهَا فِي شَكٍّ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّمَا سَلَّطْنَاهُ عَلَيْهِمْ ليظهرَ أَمْرُ مَنْ هُوَ مُؤْمِنٌ بِالْآخِرَةِ وَقِيَامِهَا وَالْحِسَابِ فِيهَا وَالْجَزَاءِ، فيُحسِنَ عِبَادَةَ رَبِّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ فِي الدُّنْيَا، مِمَّنْ هُوَ مِنْهَا فِي شَكٍّ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَرَبُّكَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ حَفِيظٌ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَعَ حِفْظِهِ ضَلّ مَنْ ضَلّ مِنَ اتِّبَاعِ إِبْلِيسَ، وَبِحِفْظِهِ وَكِلَاءَتِهِ سَلِم مَنْ سَلِمَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَتْبَاعِ الرُّسُلِ.

---

## 34:22-23 — verses 22-23 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted be He, made clear that He is the one God, the Unique, the Single, the Samad (the one depended upon absolutely, in every sense that word carries), who has no equal and no partner. Rather, He alone is self-sufficient in command, with no partner, no rival, and no opponent. So He said: {Say: Call upon those whom you claimed [as gods] besides God}, meaning, from among the deities that were worshipped besides Him, {they possess not so much as the weight of an atom in the heavens or on the earth}, just as He, blessed and exalted, said: {And those whom you call upon besides Him possess not even the skin of a date stone} [Fatir: 13].

His saying, {and they have no share in [either of] them}, means, they possess nothing, neither independently nor by way of partnership. {And He has no need of any supporter among them}, means, God has no supporter among these rivals to lean upon in [His] affairs. Rather, all creation is in need of Him, all are His servants.

Qatadah said regarding His saying, {and He has no need of any supporter among them}: no helper who assists Him with anything.

He said: {And intercession does not benefit [anyone] with Him except for one to whom He has given permission}, meaning, because of His greatness, [His majesty], and His grandeur, no one dares to intercede with Him, exalted be He, in any matter except after He has given him permission to intercede, just as He, exalted be He, said: {Who is it that can intercede with Him except by His permission?} [al-Baqarah: 255], and He said: {And how many angels are there in the heavens whose intercession avails nothing except after God gives permission to whomever He wills [and is pleased with]} [al-Najm: 26], and He said: {And they do not intercede except for one whom He approves, and they are apprehensive out of fear of Him} [al-Anbiya: 28].

For this reason it is established in the two Sahihs, through more than one route, from the Messenger of God ﷺ, who is the master of the children of Adam and the greatest intercessor before God, that when he stands at the praiseworthy station to intercede for all of creation, that their Lord may come to render final judgment, he said: "So I will prostrate to God, and He will leave me as long as God wills to leave me, and He will open to me praises which I cannot enumerate now. Then it will be said: O Muhammad, raise your head, and speak, you will be heard; ask, you will be given; intercede, your intercession will be accepted." The hadith in full.

His saying, {until, when the terror is lifted from their hearts, they say, 'What did your Lord say?' They say, 'The truth'}. This too is a lofty station regarding [God's] greatness. It means that when He, exalted be He, speaks the revelation, the inhabitants of the heavens hear His speech and tremble from awe until something like a swoon overtakes them. This was said by Ibn Mas'ud, Masruq, and others.

{Until, when the terror is lifted from their hearts}, means, when the terror departs from them. Ibn Abbas, Ibn Umar, Abu Abd al-Rahman al-Sulami, al-Sha'bi, Ibrahim al-Nakha'i, al-Dahhak, al-Hasan, and Qatadah said regarding His saying, {until, when the terror is lifted from their hearts}: it means, it is dispelled from their hearts. Some of the early scholars read it, and this has come through a marfu' (elevated) report, as "until it is emptied", with a ghayn (rather than a fa), which returns to the same first meaning.

When that occurs, some of them ask others: "What did your Lord say?" And the bearers of the Throne inform those nearest to them of that, then those nearest to them inform those beneath them, until the report reaches the inhabitants of the lowest heaven. For this reason He said, {they say, 'The truth'}, meaning, they report what He said without addition or subtraction, {and He is the Most High, the Most Great}.

Others said: rather, the meaning of His saying, {until, when the terror is lifted from their hearts}, refers to the polytheists at the moment of death, and on the Day of Resurrection, when they awaken from the heedlessness in which they had been in this world, and their reason returns to them on the Day of Resurrection, they say: "What did your Lord say?" And it is said to them: "The truth," and they are informed of that which they had been oblivious to in the world.

Ibn Abi Najih said, from Mujahid: {until, when the terror is lifted from their hearts}: the veil is removed from them on the Day of Resurrection.

Al-Hasan said: {until, when the terror is lifted from their hearts} means, what was in them of doubt and denial. Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: {until, when the terror is lifted from their hearts} means, what was in them of doubt. He said: the terror of Satan is lifted from their hearts, and he departs from them, along with their false hopes and that by which he used to lead them astray. {They say, 'What did your Lord say?' They say, 'The truth, and He is the Most High, the Most Great'}. He said: this concerns the children of Adam, this is at the time of death, when they acknowledge [the truth] at a time when acknowledgment no longer benefits them.

Ibn Jarir preferred the first view, that the pronoun refers back to the angels. This is the truth about which there is no doubt, due to the soundness of the hadiths and reports concerning it. Let us mention some of them which point to the rest:

Al-Bukhari said, when interpreting this noble verse in his Sahih: [chain] Al-Humaydi told us, Sufyan told us, Amr told us, I heard Ikrimah, I heard Abu Hurayrah say: that the Prophet of God ﷺ said: "When God decrees a matter in heaven, the angels beat their wings in submission to His word, as if it were a chain [dragged] upon a smooth rock. Then, when the terror is lifted from their hearts, they say: 'What did your Lord say?' They say to the one who spoke: 'The truth, and He is the Most High, the Most Great.' Then the one who eavesdrops hears it, and the eavesdroppers, [positioned] some above others, and Sufyan described with his hand, tilting it and spreading his fingers apart, [and one of them] hears the word and casts it down to the one below him, then the next one casts it down to the one below him, until he casts it upon the tongue of the sorcerer or the soothsayer. Sometimes the shooting flame catches him before he casts it down, and sometimes he casts it down before it catches him, so he lies along with it a hundred lies. Then it is said: 'Did he not tell us on such and such a day such and such a thing?' So [the people] believe him because of that one word which was heard from heaven."

Al-Bukhari alone transmitted this, without Muslim, by this route. Abu Dawud, al-Tirmidhi, and Ibn Majah also related it, from the hadith of Sufyan ibn Uyaynah, through him.

Another hadith: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Ja'far and Abd al-Razzaq told us: Ma'mar informed us, al-Zuhri informed us, from Ali ibn al-Husayn, from Ibn Abbas, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ was [sitting] among a group of his companions, Abd al-Razzaq said "from the Ansar", and a star was thrown [across the sky] and lit up brightly. [He said]: "What did you used to say when something like this happened in the Age of Ignorance?" They said: "We used to say a great man is born, or a great man has died." I said to al-Zuhri: "Were such [stars] thrown in the Age of Ignorance?" He said: "Yes, but it became more intense when the Prophet ﷺ was sent." He said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "It is not thrown for the death of anyone nor for his life, but rather our Lord, blessed and exalted, when He decrees a matter, the bearers of the Throne glorify Him, [then the inhabitants of the heaven nearest to them glorify Him, until the glorification reaches this world's [heaven], then the inhabitants of the heaven nearest the bearers of the Throne ask, and those nearest the bearers of the Throne say to the bearers of the Throne]: 'What did your Lord say?' And they inform them, and the inhabitants of each heaven inform [the heaven below], until the report reaches this [lowest] heaven, and the jinn snatch at the hearing and are struck down [by shooting flames]. So whatever they bring in its true form is correct, but they insert falsehoods into it and add to it."

Thus Imam Ahmad related it. Muslim also included it in his Sahih, from the hadith of Salih ibn Kaysan, al-Awza'i, Yunus, and Ma'qil ibn Ubaydullah, all four of them from al-Zuhri, from Ali ibn al-Husayn, from Ibn Abbas, from a man of the Ansar, through him. Yunus related it and said "from men of the Ansar." Al-Nasa'i likewise related it in "al-Tafsir" from the hadith of al-Zubaydi, from al-Zuhri, through him. Al-Tirmidhi related it therein from al-Husayn ibn Hurayth, from al-Walid ibn Muslim, from al-Awza'i, from al-Zuhri, from Ubaydullah ibn Abdullah, from Ibn Abbas, from a man of the Ansar, may God be pleased with him. And God knows best.

Another hadith: Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Awf and Ahmad ibn Mansur ibn Sayyar al-Ramadi told us, the wording being that of Muhammad ibn Awf, they said: Nu'aym ibn Hammad told us, al-Walid, that is ibn Muslim, told us, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Yazid ibn Jabir, from Abdullah ibn Abi Zakariyya, from Raja ibn Haywah, from al-Nawwas ibn Sam'an, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "When God wishes to reveal a matter of His, He speaks the revelation. When He speaks, the heavens are seized by a violent shaking, or he said, trembling, out of fear of God. When the inhabitants of the heavens hear that, they fall unconscious and fall down prostrate before God. The first of them to raise his head is Gabriel, and God speaks to him of His revelation whatever He wills. Then Gabriel proceeds with it past the angels, and every time he passes by a heaven, its angels ask him: 'What did our Lord say, O Gabriel?' And he says: 'He said the truth, and He is the Most High, the Most Great.' And they all say the same thing that Gabriel said. Then Gabriel arrives with the revelation wherever God commanded him, whether in heaven or on earth."

Ibn Jarir and Ibn Khuzaymah likewise related it, from Zakariyya ibn Aban al-Misri, from Nu'aym ibn Hammad, through him.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: I heard my father say: this hadith is not [reliably transmitted] in Syria from al-Walid ibn Muslim, may God have mercy on him.

Ibn Abi Hatim also related, from the hadith of al-Awfi, from Ibn Abbas, and from Qatadah, that both of them interpreted this verse as referring to the beginning of God's, glory be to Him, revealing to Muhammad ﷺ after the period of cessation that had existed between him and Jesus. There is no doubt that this is the most fitting interpretation of what is meant by this verse.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

بَيَّن تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ الْإِلَهُ الْوَاحِدُ الْأَحَدُ، الْفَرْدُ الصَّمَدُ، الَّذِي لَا نَظِيرَ لَهُ وَلَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، بَلْ هُوَ الْمُسْتَقِلُّ بِالْأَمْرِ وَحْدَهُ، مِنْ غَيْرِ مُشَارِكٍ وَلَا مُنَازِعٍ وَلَا مُعَارِضٍ، فَقَالَ: ﴿قُلِ ادْعُوا الَّذِينَ زَعَمْتُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْآلِهَةِ الَّتِي عُبِدَتْ مِنْ دونه ﴿لا يَمْلِكُونَ مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ فِي السَّمَوَاتِ وَلا فِي الأرْضِ﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ تَدْعُونَ مِنْ دُونِهِ مَا يَمْلِكُونَ مِنْ قِطْمِيرٍ﴾ [فَاطِرٍ: ١٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا لَهُمْ فِيهِمَا مِنْ شِرْكٍ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَمْلِكُونَ شَيْئًا اسْتِقْلَالًا وَلَا عَلَى سَبِيلِ الشَّرِكَةِ، ﴿وَمَا لَهُ مِنْهُمْ مِنْ ظَهِيرٍ﴾ أَيْ: وَلَيْسَ لِلَّهِ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْأَنْدَادِ مِنْ ظَهِيرٍ يُسْتَظْهَرُ بِهِ فِي الْأُمُورِ، بَلِ الْخَلْقُ كُلُّهُمْ فُقَرَاءُ إِلَيْهِ، عُبَيْدٌ لَدَيْهِ.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا لَهُ مِنْهُمْ مِنْ ظَهِيرٍ﴾ ، مِنْ عَوْنٍ يُعِينُهُ بِشَيْءٍ.

وَقَالَ: ﴿وَلا تَنْفَعُ الشَّفَاعَةُ عِنْدَهُ إِلا لِمَنْ أَذِنَ لَهُ﴾ أَيْ: لِعَظَمَتِهِ [وَجَلَالِهِ] وَكِبْرِيَائِهِ لَا يَجْتَرِئُ أَحَدٌ أَنْ يَشْفَعَ عِنْدَهُ تَعَالَى فِي شَيْءٍ إِلَّا بَعْدَ إِذْنِهِ لَهُ فِي الشَّفَاعَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يَشْفَعُ عِنْدَهُ إِلا بِإِذْنِهِ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ:٢٥٥] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَكَمْ مِنْ مَلَكٍ فِي السَّمَوَاتِ لَا تُغْنِي شَفَاعَتُهُمْ شَيْئًا إِلا مِنْ بَعْدِ أَنْ يَأْذَنَ اللَّهُ لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ [وَيَرْضَى ] ﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٢٦] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَلا يَشْفَعُونَ إِلا لِمَنِ ارْتَضَى وَهُمْ مِنْ خَشْيَتِهِ مُشْفِقُونَ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ٢٨] .

وَلِهَذَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ ، مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ -وَهُوَ سَيِّدُ وَلَدِ آدَمَ، وَأَكْبَرُ شَفِيعٍ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ-: أَنَّهُ حِينَ يَقُومُ الْمَقَامَ الْمَحْمُودَ لِيَشْفَعَ فِي الْخَلْقِ كُلِّهِمْ أَنْ يَأْتِيَ رَبَّهُمْ لِفَصْلِ الْقَضَاءِ، قَالَ: "فَأَسْجُدُ لِلَّهِ فَيَدَعُنِي مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يَدَعَنِي، وَيَفْتَحَ عَلَيَّ بِمَحَامِدَ لَا أُحْصِيهَا الْآنَ، ثُمَّ يُقَالُ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، ارْفَعْ رَأْسَكَ، وَقُلْ يُسمع ، وَسَلْ تُعْطَه وَاشْفَعْ تُشَفَّعْ" الْحَدِيثَ بِتَمَامِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُزِّعَ عَنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ قَالُوا مَاذَا قَالَ رَبُّكُمْ قَالُوا الْحَقَّ﴾ . وَهَذَا أَيْضًا مَقَامٌ رَفِيعٌ فِي الْعَظَمَةِ. وَهُوَ أَنَّهُ تَعَالَى إذا تكلم بالوحي، سمع أهل السموات كَلَامَهُ، أرْعدوا مِنَ الْهَيْبَةِ حَتَّى يَلْحَقَهُمْ مِثْلُ الْغَشْيِ. قَالَهُ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ وَمَسْرُوقٌ، وَغَيْرُهُمَا.

﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُزِّعَ عَنْ قُلُوبِهِم﴾ أَيْ: زَالَ الْفَزَعُ عَنْهَا. قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَابْنُ عُمَرَ وَأَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ السُّلَمِيُّ وَالشَّعْبِيُّ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعيّ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ وَالْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُزِّعَ عَنْ قُلُوبِهِم﴾ يَقُولُ: جُلِّى عَنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ، وَقَرَأَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ -وَجَاءَ مَرْفُوعًا-: " [حَتَّى] إذَا فُرِّغَ" بِالْغَيْنِ الْمُعْجَمَةِ، وَيَرْجِعُ إِلَى الْأَوَّلِ.

فَإِذَا كَانَ كَذَلِكَ يَسْأَلُ بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا: مَاذَا قَالَ رَبُّكُمْ؟ فَيُخْبِرُ بِذَلِكَ حَمَلَةُ الْعَرْشِ لِلَّذِينِ يَلُونَهُمْ، ثُمَّ الَّذِينَ يَلُونَهُمْ لِمَنْ تَحْتَهُمْ، حَتَّى يَنْتَهِيَ الْخَبَرُ إِلَى أَهْلِ السَّمَاءِ الدُّنْيَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿قَالُوا الْحَقّ﴾ أَيْ: أَخْبَرُوا بِمَا قَالَ مِنْ غَيْرِ زِيَادَةٍ وَلَا نُقْصَانٍ، ﴿وَهُوَ الْعَلِيُّ الْكَبِيرُ﴾ .

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: بَلْ مَعْنَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُزِّعَ عَنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْمُشْرِكِينَ عِنْدَ الِاحْتِضَارِ، وَيَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ إِذَا اسْتَيْقَظُوا مِمَّا كَانُوا فِيهِ مِنَ الْغَفْلَةِ فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَرَجَعَتْ إِلَيْهِمْ عُقُولُهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، قَالُوا: مَاذَا قَالَ رَبُّكُمْ؟ فَقِيلَ لَهُمْ: الْحَقُّ وَأُخْبِرُوا بِهِ مِمَّا كَانُوا عَنْهُ لَاهِينَ فِي الدُّنْيَا.

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيحٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُزِّعَ عَنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ﴾ : كَشَفَ عَنْهَا الْغِطَاءَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُزِّعَ عَنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ﴾ يَعْنِي: مَا فِيهَا مِنَ الشَّكِّ وَالتَّكْذِيبِ. وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: ﴿حَتَّى إِذَا فُزِّعَ عَنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ﴾ يَعْنِي: مَا فِيهَا مِنَ الشَّكِّ، قَالَ: فُزِّعَ الشَّيْطَانُ عَنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ وَفَارَقَهُمْ وَأَمَانِيهِمْ وَمَا كَانَ يُضِلُّهُمْ، ﴿قَالُوا مَاذَا قَالَ رَبُّكُمْ قَالُوا الْحَقَّ وَهُوَ الْعَلِيُّ الْكَبِيرُ﴾ قَالَ: وَهَذَا فِي بَنِي آدَمَ، هَذَا عِنْدَ الْمَوْتِ، أَقَرُّوا حِينَ لَا يَنْفَعُهُمُ الْإِقْرَارُ.

وَقَدِ اخْتَارَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ الْقَوْلَ الْأَوَّلَ: أَنَّ الضَّمِيرَ عَائِدٌ عَلَى الْمَلَائِكَةِ . هَذَا هُوَ الْحَقُّ الَّذِي لَا مِرْيَةَ فِيهِ، لِصِحَّةِ الْأَحَادِيثِ فِيهِ وَالْآثَارِ، وَلْنَذْكُرْ مِنْهَا طَرَفًا يَدُلُّ عَلَى غَيْرِهِ:

قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ عِنْدَ تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ فِي صَحِيحِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا الْحُمَيْدِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرٌو، سَمِعْتُ عِكْرِمة، سَمِعْتُ أَبَا هُرَيرة يَقُولُ: أَنَّ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِذَا قَضَى اللَّهُ الأمرَ فِي السَّمَاءِ، ضَرَبَتِ الْمَلَائِكَةُ بِأَجْنِحَتِهَا خُضعانًا لِقَوْلِهِ، كَأَنَّهُ سِلْسِلَةٌ عَلَى صفوانَ، فَإِذَا فُزِّع عَنْ قُلُوبِهِمْ قَالُوا: مَاذَا قَالَ رَبُّكُمْ؟ قالوا للذي قال: الحق، وهو العلي الكبير فَيَسْمَعُهَا مُسْتَرق السَّمْعِ، وَمُسْتَرِقُ السَّمْعِ -هَكَذَا بَعْضُهُ فَوْقَ بَعْضٍ-وَوَصَفَ سُفْيَانُ بِيَدِهِ-فَحَرّفها وبَدّد بَيْنَ أَصَابِعِهِ-فَيسمع الْكَلِمَةَ، فَيُلْقِيهَا إِلَى مَنْ تَحْتَهُ، ثُمَّ يُلْقِيهَا الْآخَرُ إِلَى مَنْ تَحْتَهُ، حَتَّى يلقيَها عَلَى لِسَانِ السَّاحِرِ أَوِ الْكَاهِنِ، فَربما أَدْرَكَهُ الشِّهَابُ قَبْلَ أَنْ يُلْقِيَهَا، وَرُبَّمَا أَلْقَاهَا قَبْلَ أَنْ يُدْرِكَهُ، فَيَكْذِبُ مَعَهَا مِائَةَ كَذْبَة، فيقال: أليس قد قال لنا يومَ كذا وكذا: كذا وكذا؟ فيصدق بتلك الكلمة الَّتِي سُمعت مِنَ السَّمَاءِ.

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ دُونَ مُسْلِمٍ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ. وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ عُيَيْنَةَ، بِهِ. 

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ وَعَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَر، أَخْبَرَنَا الزُّهْرِيُّ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ [جَالِسًا] فِي نَفَرٍ مِنْ أَصْحَابِهِ -قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: "مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ"-فَرُميَ بِنَجْمٍ فَاسْتَنَارَ، [قَالَ] : " مَا كُنْتُمْ تَقُولُونَ إِذَا كَانَ مثلُ هَذَا فِي الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ؟ " قَالُوا: كُنَّا نَقُولُ يُولَد عَظِيمٌ، أَوْ يَمُوتُ عَظِيمٌ -قُلْتُ لِلزُّهْرِيِّ: أَكَانَ يُرْمَى بِهَا فِي الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ، وَلَكِنْ غُلّظت حِينَ بُعِثَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ -قَالَ: فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "فَإِنَّهَا لَا يُرْمَى بِهَا لِمَوْتِ أَحَدٍ وَلَا لِحَيَاتِهِ، وَلَكِنَّ رَبَّنَا، تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى، إِذَا قَضَى أَمْرًا سَبَّحَ حَمَلةُ الْعَرْشِ [ثُمَّ سَبَّحَ أَهْلُ السَّمَاءِ الَّذِينَ يَلُونَهُمْ، حَتَّى يَبْلُغَ التَّسْبِيحَ هَذِهِ الدُّنْيَا، ثُمَّ يَسْتَخْبِرُ أَهْلُ السَّمَاءِ الَّذِينَ يَلُونَ حَمَلَةَ الْعَرْشِ، فَيَقُولُ الَّذِينَ يَلُونُ حَمَلَةَ الْعَرْشِ لِحَمَلَةِ الْعَرْشِ] : مَاذَا قَالَ رَبُّكُمْ؟ فَيُخْبِرُونَهُمْ، وَيُخْبِرُ أَهْلُ كُلِّ سَمَاءٍ سَمَاءً؛ حَتَّى يَنْتَهِيَ الْخَبَرُ إِلَى هَذِهِ السَّمَاءِ، وَتَخْطَفُ الْجِنُّ السَّمْعَ فَيُرْمَوْنَ، فما جاؤوا بِهِ عَلَى وَجْهِهِ فَهُوَ حَقٌّ، وَلَكِنَّهُمْ يَفْرِقُونَ فِيهِ وَيَزِيدُونَ.

هَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ . وَقَدْ أَخْرَجَهُ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ صَالِحِ بن كَيْسَان، وَالْأَوْزَاعِيِّ، وَيُونُسَ ومَعْقِل بْنِ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ ، أَرْبَعَتُهُمْ عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ، عَنْ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ عَنْ رَجُلٍ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ، بِهِ . وَرَوَاهُ وَقَالَ يُونُسُ: عَنْ رِجَالٍ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ ، وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ فِي "التَّفْسِيرِ" مِنْ حَدِيثِ الزُّبَيْدِيِّ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، بِهِ . وَرَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ فِيهِ عَنِ الحُسَين بْنِ حُرَيْثٍ؛ عَنِ الْوَلِيدِ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنِ الْأَوْزَاعِيِّ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عُبَيد اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، عَنْ رَجُلٍ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ ، واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

حَدِيثٌ آخَرُ: قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَوْفٍ وَأَحْمَدُ بْنُ مَنْصُورِ بْنِ سَيَّارٍ الرَّمَادِيُّ -وَالسِّيَاقُ لِمُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَوْفٍ-قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا نُعَيْمُ بْنُ حَمَّادٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ -هُوَ ابْنُ مُسْلِمٍ-عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ بْنِ جَابِرٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي زَكَرِيَّاءَ، عَنْ رَجَاءِ بْنِ حَيْوَةَ، عَنِ النَّوَّاسِ بْنِ سَمْعان قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا أَرَادَ اللَّهُ أَنْ يُوحِيَ بِأَمْرِهِ تَكَلَّمَ بِالْوَحْيِ، فَإِذَا تكلم أخذت السموات مِنْهُ رَجْفَةٌ -أَوْ قَالَ: رِعْدَةٌ-شَدِيدَةٌ؛ مِنْ خوف الله، فإذا سمع بذلك أهل السموات صَعِقُوا وَخَرُّوا لِلَّهِ سُجَّدًا، فَيَكُونُ أَوَّلُ مَنْ يَرْفَعُ رَأْسَهُ جِبْرِيلُ فَيُكَلِّمُهُ اللَّهُ مِنْ وَحْيِهِ بِمَا أَرَادَ، فَيَمْضِي بِهِ جِبْرِيلُ عَلَى الْمَلَائِكَةِ، كُلَّمَا مَرّ بِسَمَاءٍ سَمَاءٍ سَأَلَهُ مَلَائِكَتُهَا: مَاذَا قَالَ رَبُّنَا يَا جِبْرِيلُ؟ فَيَقُولُ: قَالَ: الْحَقُّ، وَهُوَ الْعَلِيُّ الْكَبِيرُ. فَيَقُولُونَ كُلُّهُمْ مِثْلَ مَا قَالَ جِبْرِيلُ، فَيَنْتَهِي جِبْرِيلُ بِالْوَحْيِ حَيْثُ أَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ".

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَابْنُ خُزَيمة، عَنْ زَكَرِيَّا بْنِ أَبَانٍ الْمِصْرِيِّ، عَنْ نُعَيْمِ بْنِ حَمَّادٍ، بِهِ. 

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: سَمِعْتُ أَبِي يَقُولُ: لَيْسَ هَذَا الْحَدِيثُ بِالشَّامِ عَنِ الْوَلِيدِ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ العَوفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ -وَعَنْ قَتَادَةَ: أَنَّهُمَا فَسَرَّا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ بِابْتِدَاءِ إِيحَاءِ اللَّهِ سُبْحَانَهُ إِلَى مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ بَعْدَ الْفَتْرَةِ الَّتِي كَانَتْ بَيْنَهُ وَبَيْنَ عِيسَى، وَلَا شَكَّ أَنَّ هَذَا أَوْلَى مَا دخل في هذه الآية.

---

## 34:24-27 — verses 24-27 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, establishing His sole possession of creation and provision, and His sole possession of divinity as well: just as they used to acknowledge that none provides for them from the sky and the earth, that is, through what He sends down of rain and what He causes to grow of crops, except Allah, so too let them know that there is no deity other than Him.

His saying, {And indeed, we or you are surely upon guidance or in manifest error}: this is from the style of "distribution and division" (al-laff wa al-nashr, a rhetorical device where paired items are stated together and their attributes distributed separately), meaning: one of the two parties is upon falsehood and the other is upon truth. There is no possibility that both you and we could be upon guidance, or both upon error. Rather, one of us is correct, and we have established the proof for monotheism, which shows the falsehood of the association with Allah that you practice. This is why He said: {And indeed, we or you are surely upon guidance or in manifest error}.

Qatadah said: the companions of Muhammad ﷺ said this to the polytheists: "By Allah, we and you are not upon one and the same matter. Indeed one of the two groups is surely guided."

Ikrimah and Ziyad ibn Abi Maryam said: its meaning is, "Indeed we are surely upon guidance, and you are surely in manifest error."

His saying, {Say: you will not be asked about what we have committed, nor will we be asked about what you do}: its meaning is disavowal of them, that is: you are not from us and we are not from you. Rather, we call you to Allah and to His oneness and to devoting worship to Him alone. If you respond, then you are of us and we are of you. But if you deny, then we are free of you and you are free of us, just as the Almighty said: {And if they deny you, then say, "For me are my deeds and for you are your deeds. You are disassociated from what I do, and I am disassociated from what you do"} [Yunus: 41]. And He said: {Say, O disbelievers. I do not worship what you worship. Nor are you worshippers of what I worship. Nor will I be a worshipper of what you have worshipped. Nor will you be worshippers of what I worship. For you is your religion, and for me is my religion} [Surat al-Kafirun].

His saying, {Say: our Lord will bring us together}, that is, on the Day of Resurrection, He will gather the creatures together upon one plain, then He will judge between us in truth, meaning He will decide between us with justice, rewarding every doer according to his deeds: if good, then good, and if evil, then evil. And you will know on that day to whom belong might, victory, and everlasting happiness, just as the Almighty said: {And on the Day the Hour arrives, that Day they will become divided. As for those who believed and did righteous deeds, they will be in a garden delighted. But as for those who disbelieved and denied Our signs and the meeting of the Hereafter, those will be brought into the punishment} [al-Rum: 14-16]. This is why the Almighty said: {And He is the Judge (al-Fattah, the One who opens/judges), the All-Knowing}, meaning: the just Judge, knowing the realities of all matters.

His saying, {Say: show me those whom you have attached to Him as partners}, meaning: show me these gods which you have made as rivals to Allah and set up as His equals. {No indeed}, meaning: He has no like, no rival, no partner, and no equal. This is why He said: {Rather, He is Allah}, meaning: the One, the Unique, who has no partner, {the Mighty, the Wise}, meaning: possessor of might by which He has overpowered everything and prevailed over everything, wise in His actions and His words, in His legislation and His decree. Exalted and sanctified is He.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُقَرِّرًا تفرُّدَه بِالْخَلْقِ وَالرِّزْقِ ، وَانْفِرَادَهُ بِالْإِلَهِيَّةِ أَيْضًا، فَكَمَا كَانُوا يَعْتَرِفُونَ بِأَنَّهُ لَا يَرْزُقُهُمْ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ -أَيْ: بِمَا يُنْزِلُ مِنَ الْمَطَرِ وَيُنْبِتُ مِنَ الزَّرْعِ-إِلَّا اللَّهُ، فَكَذَلِكَ فَلْيَعْلَمُوا أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ غَيْرَهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَإِنَّا أَوْ إِيَّاكُمْ لَعَلَى هُدًى أَوْ فِي ضَلالٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ : هَذَا مِنْ بَابِ اللَّفِّ وَالنَّشْرِ، أَيْ: وَاحِدٌ مِنَ الْفَرِيقَيْنِ مُبْطِلٌ، وَالْآخَرُ مُحِقٌّ، لَا سَبِيلَ إِلَى أَنْ تَكُونُوا أَنْتُمْ وَنَحْنُ عَلَى الْهُدَى أَوْ عَلَى الضَّلَالِ، بَلْ وَاحِدٌ مِنَّا مُصِيبٌ، وَنَحْنُ قَدْ أَقَمْنَا الْبُرْهَانَ عَلَى التَّوْحِيدِ، فَدَلَّ عَلَى بُطْلَانِ مَا أَنْتُمْ عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الشِّرْكِ بِاللَّهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَإِنَّا أَوْ إِيَّاكُمْ لَعَلَى هُدًى أَوْ فِي ضَلالٍ مُبِينٍ﴾ .

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: قَدْ قَالَ ذَلِكَ أَصْحَابُ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ لِلْمُشْرِكِينَ: وَاللَّهِ مَا نَحْنُ وَإِيَّاكُمْ عَلَى أَمْرٍ وَاحِدٍ، إِنَّ أَحَدَ الْفَرِيقَيْنِ لَمُهْتَدٍ.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمة وَزِيَادُ بْنُ أَبِي مَرْيَمَ: مَعْنَاهُ: إِنَّا نَحْنُ لَعَلَى هُدًى، وَإِنَّكُمْ لَفِي ضَلَالٍ مُبِينٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قُلْ لَا تُسْأَلُونَ عَمَّا أَجْرَمْنَا وَلا نُسْأَلُ عَمَّا تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ : مَعْنَاهُ التَّبَرِّي مِنْهُمْ، أَيْ: لَسْتُمْ مِنَّا وَلَا نَحْنُ مِنْكُمْ، بَلْ نَدْعُوكُمْ إِلَى اللَّهِ وَإِلَى تَوْحِيدِهِ وَإِفْرَادِ الْعِبَادَةِ لَهُ، فَإِنْ أَجَبْتُمْ فَأَنْتُمْ مِنَّا وَنَحْنُ مِنْكُمْ، وَإِنْ كَذَّبْتُمْ فَنَحْنُ بُرَآءُ مِنْكُمْ وَأَنْتُمْ بُرآء مِنَّا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنْ كَذَّبُوكَ فَقُلْ لِي عَمَلِي وَلَكُمْ عَمَلُكُمْ أَنْتُمْ بَرِيئُونَ مِمَّا أَعْمَلُ وَأَنَا بَرِيءٌ مِمَّا تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [يُونُسَ: ٤١] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿قُلْ يَا أَيُّهَا الْكَافِرُونَ. لَا أَعْبُدُ مَا تَعْبُدُونَ. وَلا أَنْتُمْ عَابِدُونَ مَا أَعْبُدُ. وَلا أَنَا عَابِدٌ مَا عَبَدْتُمْ. وَلا أَنْتُمْ عَابِدُونَ مَا أَعْبُدُ. لَكُمْ دِينُكُمْ وَلِيَ دِينِ﴾ [سُورَةُ الْكَافِرُونَ] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قُلْ يَجْمَعُ بَيْنَنَا رَبُّنَا﴾ أَيْ: يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، يَجْمَعُ [بَيْنَ] الْخَلَائِقِ فِي صَعِيدٍ وَاحِدٍ، ثُمَّ يَفْتَحُ بَيْنَنَا بِالْحَقِّ، أَيْ: يَحْكُمُ بَيْنَنَا بِالْعَدْلِ، فَيَجْزِي كُلَّ عَامِلٍ بِعَمَلِهِ، إِنْ خَيْرًا فَخَيْرٌ، وَإِنْ شَرًّا فَشَرٌّ. وَسَتَعْلَمُونَ يَوْمَئِذٍ لِمَنِ الْعِزَّةُ وَالنُّصْرَةُ وَالسَّعَادَةُ الْأَبَدِيَّةُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيَوْمَ تَقُومُ السَّاعَةُ يَوْمَئِذٍ يَتَفَرَّقُونَ. فَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ فَهُمْ فِي رَوْضَةٍ يُحْبَرُونَ. وَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَكَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا وَلِقَاءِ الآخِرَةِ فَأُولَئِكَ فِي الْعَذَابِ مُحْضَرُونَ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ١٤-١٦] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَهُوَ الْفَتَّاحُ الْعَلِيمُ﴾ أَيِ: الْحَاكِمُ الْعَادِلُ الْعَالِمُ بِحَقَائِقِ الْأُمُورِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿قُلْ أَرُونِيَ الَّذِينَ أَلْحَقْتُمْ بِهِ شُرَكَاءَ﴾ أَيْ: أَرَوْنِي هَذِهِ الْآلِهَةِ الَّتِي جَعَلْتُمُوهَا لِلَّهِ أَنْدَادًا وصيَّرتموها لَهُ عدْلا. ﴿كَلا﴾ أَيْ: لَيْسَ لَهُ نَظِيرٌ وَلَا نَديد، وَلَا شَرِيكٌ وَلَا عَدِيلٌ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿بَلْ هُوَ اللَّهُ﴾ :أَيِ: الْوَاحِدُ الْأَحَدُ الَّذِي لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ ﴿الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ﴾ أَيْ: ذُو الْعِزَّةِ الَّتِي قَدْ قهر بِهَا كُلَّ شَيْءٍ، وَغَلَبت كُلَّ شَيْءٍ، الْحَكِيمُ فِي أَفْعَالِهِ وَأَقْوَالِهِ، وَشَرْعِهِ وَقَدَرِهِ، تَعَالَى وَتَقَدَّسَ.

---

## 34:28-30 — verses 28-30 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says to His servant and messenger Muhammad, may the prayers and peace of Allah be upon him: {And We have not sent you except to all of mankind}, meaning: except to all created beings who are subject to divine obligation, as in His saying: {Say: O mankind, indeed I am the messenger of Allah to you all} [al-A'raf: 158], and {Blessed is He who sent down the Criterion upon His servant that he may be a warner to the worlds} [al-Furqan: 1]. {A bringer of glad tidings and a warner}, meaning: you give glad tidings to whoever obeys you of Paradise, and you warn whoever disobeys you of the Fire.

{But most of mankind do not know}, as in His saying: {And most of mankind, even if you desire it eagerly, are not believers} [Yusuf: 103], and {And if you obey most of those upon the earth, they will lead you astray from the path of Allah} [al-An'am: 116].

Muhammad ibn Ka'b said concerning His saying, {And We have not sent you except to all of mankind}: meaning, to mankind universally.

Qatadah said regarding this verse: Allah sent Muhammad ﷺ to the Arabs and the non-Arabs, and the most honored of them before Allah is the most obedient of them to Allah, Mighty and Majestic.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ikrimah said: I heard Ibn Abbas say: Allah favored Muhammad ﷺ over the people of heaven and over the prophets. They said: O Ibn Abbas, in what did Allah favor him over the prophets? He said: Allah said, {And We have not sent any messenger except in the language of his people, that he might make things clear to them}, and He said to the Prophet ﷺ: {And We have not sent you except to all of mankind}. So Allah sent him to the jinn and to mankind.

This statement of Ibn Abbas has been established as raised to the Prophet ﷺ in the two Sahihs, on the authority of Jabir, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I have been given five things which no prophet before me was given: I was aided by terror striking my enemies from a month's distance away. The earth was made for me a place of prostration and a means of purification, so whichever man of my nation is overtaken by the time of prayer, let him pray. The spoils of war were made lawful for me, and they were not lawful for anyone before me. I was given intercession. And every prophet before me was sent to his own people, while I was sent to mankind universally."

It is also established in the Sahih that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "I was sent to the black and the red." Mujahid said this means: the jinn and mankind. Others said it means: the Arabs and the non-Arabs. Both are correct.

Then the Exalted says, reporting concerning the disbelievers in their treating the coming of the Hour as improbable: {And they say: When is this promise, if you are truthful?}

As He says elsewhere: {Those who do not believe in it seek to hasten it, while those who believe are fearful of it and know that it is the truth} [al-Shura: 18], the rest of the verse.

Then He says: {Say: For you is the appointment of a Day which you cannot delay by an hour, nor bring forward}, meaning: you have a fixed, determined, recorded appointed time, which is neither increased nor diminished, and when it comes it will not be delayed by an hour nor advanced, as He says: {Indeed, the appointed time of Allah, when it comes, is not delayed} [Nuh: 4], and He says: {And We do not delay it except for a specified term. The Day it comes, no soul will speak except by His permission, and among them will be the wretched and the fortunate} [Hud: 104, 105].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى لِعَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ مُحَمَّدٍ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ : ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ إِلا كَافَّةً لِلنَّاسِ ﴾ : أَيْ: إِلَّا إِلَى جَمِيعِ الْخَلْقِ مِنَ الْمُكَلَّفِينَ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ إِنِّي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ إِلَيْكُمْ جَمِيعًا﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٥٨] ، ﴿تَبَارَكَ الَّذِي نزلَ الْفُرْقَانَ عَلَى عَبْدِهِ لِيَكُونَ لِلْعَالَمِينَ نَذِيرًا﴾ [الْفُرْقَانِ: ١] . ﴿بَشِيرًا وَنَذِيرًا﴾ أَيْ تُبَشِّرُ مَنْ أَطَاعَكَ بِالْجَنَّةِ، وَتُنْذِرُ مَنْ عَصَاكَ بِالنَّارِ.

﴿وَلَكِنَّ أَكْثَرَ النَّاسِ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ﴾ ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا أَكْثَرُ النَّاسِ وَلَوْ حَرَصْتَ بِمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ [يُوسُفَ: ١٠٣] ، ﴿وَإِنْ تُطِعْ أَكْثَرَ مَنْ فِي الأرْضِ يُضِلُّوكَ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١١٦] .

قَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ إِلا كَافَّةً لِلنَّاسِ﴾ يَعْنِي: إِلَى النَّاسِ عَامَّةً.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: أَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ مُحَمَّدًا ﷺ إِلَى الْعَرَبِ وَالْعَجَمِ، فأكرمُهم عَلَى اللَّهِ أَطْوَعُهُمْ لِلَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الظَّهْرَانِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا حَفْصُ بْنُ عُمَرَ العَدَني، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَكَمُ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ أَبَانٍ -عَنْ عِكْرِمة قَالَ: سَمِعْتُ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ يَقُولُ: إِنِ اللَّهَ فَضَّلَ مُحَمَّدًا ﷺ عَلَى أَهْلِ السَّمَاءِ وعلى الأنبياء. قالوا: يا بن عَبَّاسٍ، فِيمَ فَضَّلَهُ اللَّهُ عَلَى الْأَنْبِيَاءِ؟ قَالَ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ قَالَ: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلا بِلِسَانِ قَوْمِهِ لِيُبَيِّنَ لَهُمْ﴾ ، وَقَالَ لِلنَّبِيِّ ﷺ: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ إِلا كَافَّةً لِلنَّاسِ﴾ ، فَأَرْسَلَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَى الْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ.

وَهَذَا الَّذِي قَالَهُ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ قَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ رَفْعهُ عَنْ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أُعْطِيتُ خَمْسًا لَمْ يُعْطَهُنَّ أَحَدٌ مِنَ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ قَبْلِي: نُصِرْتُ بِالرُّعْبِ مَسِيرَةَ شَهْرٍ. وَجُعِلَتْ لِيَ الْأَرْضُ مَسْجِدًا وَطَهُورًا، فَأَيُّمَا رَجُلٌ مِنْ أُمَّتِي أَدْرَكَتْهُ الصَّلَاةُ فَلْيُصَلِّ. وَأُحِلَّتْ لِيَ الْغَنَائِمُ، وَلَمْ تَحِلَّ لِأَحَدٍ قَبْلِي. وَأُعْطِيتُ الشَّفَاعَةَ. وَكَانَ النَّبِيُّ يُبْعَثُ إِلَى قَوْمِهِ، وَبُعِثْتُ إِلَى النَّاسِ عَامَّةً". 

وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ أَيْضًا أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "بُعِثْتُ إِلَى الْأَسْوَدِ وَالْأَحْمَرِ" : قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ. يَعْنِي: الْجِنَّ وَالْإِنْسَ. وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُ: يَعْنِي: الْعَرَبَ وَالْعَجَمَ. وَالْكُلُّ صَحِيحٌ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى مُخْبِرًا عَنِ الْكُفَّارِ فِي اسْتِبْعَادِهِمْ قِيَامَ السَّاعَةِ: ﴿وَيَقُولُونَ مَتَى هَذَا الْوَعْدُ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ﴾

، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَسْتَعْجِلُ بِهَا الَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِهَا وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مُشْفِقُونَ مِنْهَا وَيَعْلَمُونَ أَنَّهَا الْحَقُّ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الشُّورَى: ١٨] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ: ﴿قُلْ لَكُمْ مِيعَادُ يَوْمٍ لَا تَسْتَأْخِرُونَ عَنْهُ سَاعَةً وَلا تَسْتَقْدِمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَكُمْ مِيعَادٌ مُؤَجَّلٌ مَعْدُودٌ مُحَرَّرٌ، لَا يَزْدَادُ وَلَا يَنْتَقِصُ، فَإِذَا جَاءَ فَلَا يُؤَخَّرُ سَاعَةً وَلَا يُقَدَّمُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ أَجَلَ اللَّهِ إِذَا جَاءَ لَا يُؤَخَّرُ﴾ [نُوحٍ: ٤] ، وَقَالَ ﴿وَمَا نُؤَخِّرُهُ إِلا لأجَلٍ مَعْدُودٍ. يَوْمَ يَأْتِ لَا تَكَلَّمُ نَفْسٌ إِلا بِإِذْنِهِ فَمِنْهُمْ شَقِيٌّ وَسَعِيدٌ﴾ [هُودٍ: ١٠٤، ١٠٥] .

---

## 34:31-33 — verses 31-33 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty informs us of the disbelievers' persistence in their transgression and obstinacy, and their insistence upon not believing in the Qur'an and what it reports concerning the resurrection. Hence He said: {And those who disbelieved said, "We will never believe in this Qur'an, nor in that which came before it."} God the Almighty then speaks with threat and warning toward them, informing of their humiliated positions before Him at the time of their mutual disputing and arguing: {They will turn the discourse back and forth between themselves.} {Those who were deemed weak}, meaning the followers among them, will say {to those who were arrogant}, meaning their leaders and chiefs: {"Had it not been for you, we would have been believers."} That is: had you not obstructed us, we would have followed the messengers and believed in what they brought us. The leaders and chiefs, who were the arrogant ones, then said to them: {"Did we bar you from guidance after it had come to you?"} That is: we did nothing to you beyond calling you, and you followed us without proof or evidence, and you opposed the proofs, evidences, and arguments that the prophets brought, out of your own desire and your own choice to do so. Hence they said: {"Rather, you yourselves were criminals."} {And those who were deemed weak will say to those who were arrogant, "Rather, it was your scheming by night and day."} That is: rather, you were scheming against us night and day, deceiving us and making us hope for false things, telling us that we were upon guidance and upon something worthwhile, when in fact all of that was falsehood, lies, and deceit.

Qatada and Ibn Zayd said regarding {"Rather, it was your scheming by night and day"}: it means, rather, their scheming by night and day. Malik said likewise, from Zayd ibn Aslam: their scheming by night and day.

{"When you commanded us to disbelieve in God and to set up rivals to Him,"} meaning equals and deities alongside Him, and you presented us with specious arguments and impossible things by which you led us astray. {And they concealed their remorse when they saw the punishment}, meaning all of them, the chiefs and the followers alike, each one regretting what he had done before.

{And We placed shackles upon the necks of those who disbelieved}: these are the chains that bind their hands together with their necks. {Are they rewarded except for what they used to do?} That is: We only repay you according to your deeds, each according to his measure. The leaders will have punishment according to their measure, and the followers according to theirs. {He will say, "For each is a double punishment, but you do not know"} [al-A'raf: 38].

Ibn Abi Hatim said: my father narrated to us, Farwa ibn Abi al-Mighra' narrated to us, Muhammad ibn Sulayman ibn al-Asbahani narrated to us, from Abu Sinan Dirar ibn Surad, from Abdullah ibn Abi al-Hudhayl, from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "When Hell's people are driven toward it, its flame will meet them, then it will scorch them with a single scorching, so that no flesh will remain except that it falls off down to the heel bone."

My father also narrated to us: Ahmad ibn Abi al-Hawari narrated to us, al-Tayyib Abu al-Hasan narrated to us, from al-Hasan ibn Yahya al-Khushani, who said: there is no dwelling in Hell, nor cavern, nor shackle, nor chain, nor fetter, except that the name of its owner is written upon it. He said: I related this to Abu Sulayman, meaning al-Darani, may God's mercy be upon him, and he wept, then said: woe unto you! How would it be for him if all of this were gathered upon him at once: the fetter placed upon his legs, the shackle upon his hands, the chain around his neck, and then he were made to enter the Fire and made to enter the cavern as well?!

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ تَمَادِي الْكُفَّارِ فِي طُغْيَانِهِمْ وَعِنَادِهِمْ وَإِصْرَارِهِمْ عَلَى عَدَمِ الْإِيمَانِ بِالْقُرْآنِ وَمَا أَخْبَرَ بِهِ مِنْ أَمْرِ الْمَعَادِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لَنْ نُؤْمِنَ بِهَذَا الْقُرْآنِ وَلا بِالَّذِي بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ﴾ . قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى مُتَهَدِّدًا لَهُمْ وَمُتَوَعِّدًا، وَمُخْبِرًا عَنْ مَوَاقِفِهِمُ الذَّلِيلَةِ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ فِي حَالِ تُخَاصِمِهِمْ وَتَحَاجِّهِمْ: ﴿يَرْجِعُ بَعْضُهُمْ إِلَى بَعْضٍ الْقَوْلَ يَقُولُ الَّذِينَ اسْتُضْعِفُوا﴾ مِنْهُمْ وَهُمُ الْأَتْبَاعُ ﴿لِلَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا﴾ وَهُمْ قَادَتُهُمْ وَسَادَتُهُمْ: ﴿لَوْلا أَنْتُمْ لَكُنَّا مُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ أَيْ: لَوْلَا أَنْتُمْ تَصُدُّونَا، لَكُنَّا اتَّبَعْنَا الرُّسُلَ وَآمَنَّا بِمَا جاؤونا بِهِ. فَقَالَ لَهُمُ الْقَادَةُ وَالسَّادَةُ، وَهُمُ الَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا: ﴿أَنَحْنُ صَدَدْنَاكُمْ عَنِ الْهُدَى بَعْدَ إِذْ جَاءَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: نَحْنُ مَا فَعَلْنَا بِكُمْ أَكْثَرَ مِنْ أنَّا دَعَوْنَاكُمْ فَاتَّبَعْتُمُونَا مِنْ غَيْرِ دَلِيلٍ وَلَا بُرْهَانٍ، وَخَالَفْتُمُ الْأَدِلَّةَ وَالْبَرَاهِينَ وَالْحُجَجَ الَّتِي جَاءَتْ بِهَا الْأَنْبِيَاءُ، لِشَهْوَتِكُمْ وَاخْتِيَارِكُمْ لِذَلِكَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالُوا: ﴿بَلْ كُنْتُمْ مُجْرِمِينَ. وَقَالَ الَّذِينَ اسْتُضْعِفُوا لِلَّذِينَ اسْتَكْبَرُوا بَلْ مَكْرُ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَار﴾ أَيْ: بَلْ كُنْتُمْ تَمْكُرُونَ بِنَا لَيْلًا وَنَهَارًا، وتَغُرّونا وتُمَنّونا، وَتُخْبِرُونَا أَنَّا عَلَى هُدًى وَأَنَّا عَلَى شَيْءٍ، فَإِذَا جَمِيعُ ذَلِكَ بَاطِلٌ وكَذبٌ ومَيْن.

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ، وَابْنُ زَيْدٍ : ﴿بَلْ مَكْرُ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ﴾ يَقُولُ: بَلْ مَكْرُهُمْ بِاللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ مَالِكٌ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: مَكْرُهُمْ بِاللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ.

﴿إِذْ تَأْمُرُونَنَا أَنْ نَكْفُرَ بِاللَّهِ وَنَجْعَلَ لَهُ أَنْدَادًا﴾ أَيْ نُظَرَاءَ وَآلِهَةً مَعَهُ، وتقيموا لنا شُبَهًا وأشياءَ من الْمُحَالِ تُضِلُّونَا بِهَا ﴿وَأَسَرُّوا النَّدَامَةَ لَمَّا رَأَوُا الْعَذَابَ﴾ أَيِ: الْجَمِيعُ مِنَ السَّادَةِ وَالْأَتْبَاعِ، كُلٌّ نَدم عَلَى مَا سَلَف مِنْهُ.
